Li Yizhi's Letter to the Economic Council Reports the Disaster Situation in Western Shandong; The Economic Council Rents a Plane to Survey the Disaster

(Nanjing) Li Yizhi and others sent a letter to the Economic Council reporting that the disaster area in western Shandong is in the shape of a triangle. The western area is bounded by the Yellow River levee, the northeast is bounded by the Yun River, and the southwest is bounded by the Wanfu River South Levee. The flooded area is approximately 6,000 square kilometers. The Yellow River breech at Dongzhuang rushed southeast to the Wanglaohu area, then divided into three streams. One flowed northeast through Songjin River, Yuncheng, and into Dongping Lake. One flowed through Niutou River, Juye, and north of Jiaxiang into Nanwang Lake and Nanyang Lake. One flowed through Lai Shui River into Nanyang Lake and into Weishan Lake. The inland water depth in the entire province reached two to three meters, and there were many disaster victims. The Shandong Provincial Government is using civilian ships to transport the disaster victims, first to Jining, and then distributing them to various counties for organization. The Economic Council immediately rented a plane from the Eurasia Aviation Corporation and sent personnel to the disaster area to determine the extent of the flooding and the disaster situation. At 8:00 AM on the morning of the 15th, the Eurasia No. 2 aircraft flew from Beijing to Xuzhou and the western Shandong area. Those assigned to take the plane for the survey were Wu Youdun, a technician from the Water Conservancy Department, Xu Xinwu, the chief engineer of the Yellow River Committee, consultant Baker, and Director Wang and technicians from the Aviation Survey Team. After the survey was completed that afternoon, the plane returned to Beijing. The plane for the Yangtze River survey is scheduled for the 7th on the morning of the 16th. (15th Special Dispatch)

Situation of the Six Academic Organizations Meeting in Nanning

Nanning The Chinese Science Society, the Chinese Institute of Engineers, the Chemical Society, the Geographical Society, the Zoological Society, and the Botanical Society—six organizations—held a joint annual meeting at the Nanning Provincial Government Auditorium at 7:00 AM on the 12th. More than 400 members from various regions attended. Zhu Kezhen presided and performed the formalities. Third, science has no national boundaries, and people from Europe, America, and Japan have come to participate. Finally, he expressed deep gratitude to the Guangxi authorities for their warm hospitality. Subsequently, Li Zongren, Commander-in-Chief of the Fourth Group Army, and Huang Xuchu, Chairman of Guangxi Province, delivered speeches one after another, briefly stating that the arrival of the six organizations for the meeting, gathering talents, opened the newest record for Guangxi, and released unprecedented academic brilliance. Using academics to save the country will surely see great development. Guangxi Province is barren and poor, and although it is fully engaged in construction, its strength is insufficient. It is hoped that everyone will provide criticism and guidance as much as possible. Next, representatives of various organizations reported on the progress of their work. Interpretation of Implementation Issues

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan explained the ambiguity in Article 2, Paragraph 3 of the new Criminal Law as follows: After a judgment on multiple offenses has been finalized, if it has not been executed or the execution has not been completed, and one of the offenses is exempt from execution because the act is not punishable under the Criminal Law, and there are still several offenses remaining, the court should be requested to amend the sentence in accordance with Article 54 of the Criminal Law and Article 481 of the Criminal Procedure Law. If only one offense remains, it should be executed according to the heavier sentence. Furthermore, if the penalty for a minor offense in a related offense case has been absorbed by the penalty for a major offense, and the major offense with the heavier penalty is no longer punishable due to changes in the law, the execution of the penalty should be directly exempted. (Central News Agency, 15th)

Recent News on Land Registration in Nanjing

(Nanjing) Wang Shufang, Secretary-General of the Nanjing Municipality, stated that land registration procedures have been completed, and 30,000 households are required to complete the registration within the 24th year. Current Commentary

The Possibility of Success for the Three-Nation Conference

— Heng

The Three-Nation Conference of England, France, and Italy. Preparatory talks are currently underway, and the official opening is imminent. The convening of this conference was decided before the recent meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council. Since the Executive Council could not fully resolve the Italian-Abyssinian issue, it had to seek another solution outside of the League of Nations. This conference is largely based on the 1906 agreement between England, France, and Italy regarding Abyssinia and the 1925 exchange of notes between England and Italy. The former agreement superficially recognized and respected the territorial integrity of Abyssinia but was actually a contract for the three countries to prepare to divide Abyssinia's sphere of influence. The most notable point was that the agreement allowed Italy to build railways within Abyssinia. As for the 1925 exchange of notes between England and Italy, England further allowed Italy to exclusively enjoy various economic benefits along the railways. Therefore, after this meeting convenes, England will be able to meet Italy with greater sincerity and will not just pay lip service. According to recent European dispatches, England is prepared to allow Italy to acquire extensive economic benefits in Abyssinia in accordance with the conditions outlined in the 1925 exchange of notes between the two countries, but it will not recognize its political preferential rights. Although this proposal by England may not be fully accepted by Italy, it is very clear that England has returned to the position of 1925 on the Italian-Abyssinian issue. From this perspective, if this conference can succeed, the Italian-Abyssinian War may be avoided, but the independence and sovereignty of Abyssinia will inevitably suffer some harm.

The possibility of success for this conference is still unknown. However, its impact on the European situation is not insignificant. Because England's current actions demonstrate great determination, if France and Italy cannot coordinate with England, then England will withdraw from the European collective peace system and will ignore threats to France from Germany or invasions of Austria by Germany (see Paris dispatch, 14th). This step by England will cause great anxiety for France and Italy. Considering this, the two countries can increase the possibility of success for this conference. Regarding France, it strongly opposed England's proposal to Italy in 1925, believing that it went against the principles of maintaining Abyssinia's territorial integrity and open door policy in the 1906 Three-Nation Agreement (see Briand's reply to England and Italy, July 14, 1926). Recently, France has been catering to Italy's will in every way, wanting Italy to support its position against Germany. However, the establishment of a European collective peace system relies heavily on England's support. If England announces its withdrawal, France's position against Germany will be greatly threatened. Even with Italy's cooperation, it will not help. Therefore, France slightly changing its policy of assisting Italy in every way and working hard to mediate so that a Three-Nation Agreement can be established is something that France would naturally want to do. Regarding Italy, Mussolini has consistently declared his ambition to swallow the entire territory of Abyssinia. However, if the breakdown of the Three-Nation Conference results in England's withdrawal from the European collective peace system, the situation in Central Europe will change drastically. At this time, even if Italy wants to manage Abyssinia, it cannot help but be concerned. Mussolini once hinted at a strategy of joining hands with Germany, but there were two preconditions: (1) Germany recognizes Austria's independence. (2) Italy has the determination to abandon its friendship with France. Judging from the current situation, Italy joining hands with Germany would not be of much benefit. Moreover, judging from the 1925 exchange of notes between England and Italy, Italy's hope for Abyssinia was originally the same as England's proposal. If it gives up military action against Abyssinia and submits to England's proposal, it cannot be said to have lost face. Therefore, it is also possible that Italy will generally accept this British proposal.

US Treasury Secretary Reaffirms Silver Purchases Will Rise and Fall with Market Prices, Stabilizing Silver Prices and Preventing Silver Faction Activities, Over 20 Million Ounces Purchased on Wednesday

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau announced today that the Treasury Department purchased 25 million ounces of silver on Wednesday. The amount of silver purchased on this one day was even greater than the national production last year. The Treasury Secretary also said that the Treasury Department's silver purchase plan will gradually increase as silver prices fall. The Treasury Secretary also said that the purchases were made in New York and London, and that purchases will continue in the future. Morgenthau also denied rumors that he had been negligent in purchasing silver in recent days. As for what impact the government's silver purchase plan will have on the market, Morgenthau said he did not know. As for the amount of silver coins in circulation, Morgenthau thought the number had decreased slightly. (National Dispatch, 14th)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau's comments today, made after various rumors and protests from silver faction senators, are seen by many as a move to prevent the Senate from investigating silver purchase procedures and to stop the world's silver bulls from continuing to close out their positions. Morgenthau also said that when market prices are low, the Treasury Department increases silver purchases, which is a good deal. This policy makes the Treasury Department less active when prices are stable, but very active when speculators close out their positions. Recently, India and China have sold large quantities, causing world silver prices to plummet, he said. (Reuters, 14th)

London Silver Market More Stable, Result of US Treasury Secretary's Remarks

(London) The silver market was more stable this morning, which was due to US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau's statement in Washington yesterday that the United States will continue to purchase silver in order to eliminate the bulls. According to estimates, the United States has purchased approximately 50 million to 60 million ounces of silver in the past three days. The Financial Times reported that since the passage of the Silver Act, the United States has purchased a total of 38,505,000 ounces of newly mined silver, 112,912,000 ounces of nationally owned silver, and 270,000,000 ounces purchased on the open market. At the same time, the United States' gold reserves have greatly increased, so the silver holdings are not relatively large. Therefore, the ratio of one-third gold to three-thirds silver stipulated in the Silver Act is still far away. Experts estimate that if the United States no longer purchases gold from now on, it will still need to purchase 800 million ounces of silver to meet this ratio. (Reuters, 15th)

(London) All newspapers published silver news on the front page because of the huge volume of transactions. It is estimated that the United States purchased 25 million ounces from the bulls today. India and China, who were previously engaged in multiple positions, sold first in order to close out their positions because there was no new development in the US silver purchase policy. Yesterday, the United States purchased huge quantities at a slightly lower price than before. Today, seeing yesterday's price drop, the bulls rushed to sell, and the market price initially fell by one and three-quarters pence lower than yesterday, and then another quarter. The United States purchased a lot of silver and had to purchase a lot of foreign exchange, so the exchange rate of the US dollar in terms of pounds sterling was weak. The selling wind was strong yesterday and today, and the bulls' chips were greatly reduced, so the silver market showed a more stable atmosphere. (Reuters, 14th)

(New York) Wall Street believes that the continued decline in silver prices is a reflection of speculators' disappointment. Speculators feel that the Treasury Department is not maintaining silver prices and that Congress is in recess, so they expect that there will be no favorable actions for the silver faction for the time being, and they are closing out their positions one after another. There is a saying in the New York market that the Treasury Department continues to purchase, but according to silver merchants, the Treasury Department is particularly serious about delivery and timing, so the general public believes that this move by the Treasury Department makes it difficult for speculators to sell. At the same time, the parliament is silent on the low silver price. Only Senator Pittman commented on this matter, saying that he was not alarmed at all because he was sure that the Treasury Department's actions would be sure to be effective. (Reuters, 14th)

US Senate Silver Faction Plans to Propose Investigating Government Actions, Anxious About Low Silver Prices, President Approves Social Security Act

(Washington) Senate Silver Faction Leader Thomas announced today that he plans to ask the Senate Agriculture Committee to investigate the government's silver purchase policy. Thomas said that silver prices have fallen again today, so he believes that there should be action. However, neutral observers and experts here believe that there are three main reasons for the decline in silver prices: (1) Speculators believe that the Treasury Department does not want to actively purchase silver for the time being; (2) The near end of the congressional recess will gradually eliminate the pressure to urge the government to speed up silver purchases; (3) Recently, the ratio of the US dollar to the pound sterling has plummeted. At the same time, Senator McCarran has proposed an amendment to the estate tax bill to abolish the silver profit tax. If McCarran asks for a vote, the vote will be held in the middle of this week. However, McCarran said that he does not plan to ask for a vote unless he is sure of passing it. (National Dispatch, 14th)

(Washington) Democratic Senator Thomas, the leader of the Senate Silver Faction, said today that he is drafting a proposal to ask Congress to investigate the government's silver purchase procedures. The investigation is not aimed at individuals, but is related to the government's overall procedures. If the silver purchase procedures must be implemented, they should be implemented immediately, because the current government does not have a guarantee of being in power forever. If such procedures do not need to be implemented, they should also be stopped immediately and should not be delayed for a long time. (Reuters, 14th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt approved the Social Security Act today and said that this act is the cornerstone of a new building that has not yet been completed. The amazing changes in culture and industry in the past century have made life more and more insecure. Today, this act has realized a large part of many years of hope, will pay attention to human needs, and will establish a more stable economic structure in the United States. (Reuters, 14th)

(Washington) The Senate discussed President Roosevelt's estate tax bill today. Republican Senator Vandenberg moved to leave this bill for consideration at the next congressional session. As a result of the vote, Vandenberg's motion was rejected by 55 votes to 19. This was the first failure of the Republican Party to attack the current government. (National Dispatch, 14th)

(Washington) The Agricultural Adjustment Administration today reduced the wheat acreage reduction required in the 1936 wheat adjustment contract from 15% to 10%. This change will increase the US wheat acreage by 5.2 million acres in 1936. The Secretary of Agriculture told reporters that the August wheat production report showed that US wheat production was greatly reduced due to damage from black rust and hot weather. Therefore, after the release of this report, it was decided to reduce the reduction. He hoped that this move would enable the United States to stand in a strong position in the world export market. (Reuters, 14th)

(Washington) Senator Bankhead predicted today that the authorities will announce a cotton loan of 12 cents per pound around the end of this week. (Reuters, 14th)

US and Far East Economy, Asked Whether Roosevelt Will Send an Investigation Team

(Washington) Today, someone asked President Roosevelt whether the United States intended to send an economic investigation team to China. President Roosevelt turned this question over to the State Department. The reason for this question is that the United States' attitude towards the United Kingdom sending Sir Otto Niemeyer to China to investigate the economy was too cold. The US side also said that the US economic investigation team that recently returned to the US from the Far East and the private organizations that fully represent commercial groups have no relationship with the government. (National News Agency, 14th)

Philippines Asks US to Maintain Market, Allow Philippine Goods to be Freely Imported into US

(Washington) Philippine Vice Governor Hayden wrote to Senator Tydings, Chairman of the Senate Territorial Affairs Committee, saying that after a detailed study of all the facts, it is known that if Philippine products cannot continue to be freely imported into the US market in large quantities, the Philippine independent government will not have sufficient revenue to maintain the expenses of the central or local governments. The standard of living in the Philippines is much higher than in other places in the Far East, so it is difficult for its products to compete with other countries in any market except the United States. If economic difficulties occur, political unrest will naturally follow. Therefore, if the United States implements the full import tax rate on the Philippines, the experiment of the autonomous government will fail. Hayden believes that the most appropriate reciprocal trade agreement between the United States and the Philippines is to allow goods that do not compete with American agricultural and industrial products to be freely imported, while US goods are also used as trade on the same terms. At present, the United States is seeking trade all over the world, so why not maintain and promote the Philippine market? (National Dispatch, 15th)

Japanese Committee Members and Staff Decided for the Japan-Manchukuo Economic Committee

(Tokyo) The government issued an order today appointing Lieutenant General Nishio Toshizo, Embassy Counselor Tani Masayuki, Director-General of the Eastern Bureau Ono Rokuro, and Takeushi Kakichi, Fourth Rank, Third Class Order of Merit, as Japanese members of the Japan-Manchukuo Joint Economic Committee. It also appointed Embassy First Secretary Yamamoto Kumaichi, Army Infantry Colonel Nagatsu Sabiju, Army Infantry Lieutenant Colonel Akiyaga Getsuzo, and Director of the Kwantung Army Government Policy Department Takebe Rokuzo as Japanese staff members of the Japan-Manchukuo Joint Economic Committee. ((Japan Federation News, 15th)

(Tokyo) Since Matsuoka Yosuke took office as the president of South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu), he has been discussing various policies with the authorities of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Army, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Colonial Affairs. Because the work has been completed, he is scheduled to leave Tokyo on the 23rd at 9:00 AM to take office. (Japan Federation News, 15th)

(Changchun) Manchurian trade has become a deformed development in recent years, that is, since the September 18th Incident, it has changed from a surplus in previous years to a deficit. Imported goods are almost exclusively occupied by Japanese goods. In the first half of this year, Japanese goods accounted for more than 70% of import trade. Therefore, Manchuria has become an exclusive market for Japanese goods. Thousands of acres of forest land in the three states of Spokan, Mountana, Idaho and Oregon are on fire. A thousand firefighters are working hard to rescue. Wild animals in the forest, such as bears, deer, and rabbits, are being burned by the flames and are scurrying around. It is feared that many wild animals will die. (Reuters, 14th)

An investigation of the trade in the first half of this year shows that exports were 225,529,200 yuan and imports were 298,824,300 yuan. Compared to last year, not only were exports much worse, but imports also increased sharply by 30,129,000 yuan. The deficit jumped to 72,951,000 yuan. Furthermore, Japanese goods accounted for 214,255,000 yuan of the total import amount, exceeding 70% of the total amount. Now, let's look at the overall trend of Manchurian trade since 1931 before the September 18th Incident, listing the amounts (unit: thousand yuan):

1931 Surplus 39,762

1932 Surplus 280,484

1933 Deficit 67,354

1934 Deficit 145,135

1935 (Half Year) Deficit 72,950

That is, since 1933, the trade in "Manchuria" has suddenly changed from a traditional surplus to a deficit, and exports have gradually decreased and imports have gradually increased. In the first half of this year, it reached an unprecedented deficit. The most noteworthy thing is that the relationship between the import and export of Japanese goods has suddenly increased, and the impact of the deficit on the finances of "Manchuria" is also great.

The main reasons for the decline in exports are two: (1) the world agricultural panic; (2) the decline in exports to China and the severance of trade. Since the September 18th Incident, "Manchuria"'s exports have decreased by about 60%. The increase in imports is due to the influx of Japanese goods and the increase in materials such as railway construction materials exported from Japan. However, for some commodities, they have caused an increase in exports and a decrease in imports. Those that caused an increase in exports include steel, sulfur, wood, coal, wool, salt, beef, and flax. Those that caused a decrease in imports include wheat flour, cement, ironware, kerosene, beer, wood, and other cotton, sacks, and cigarettes. In short, Manchurian trade has become a deformed development in recent years and is subject to the domination of Japanese economic power. (China United Press, 15th)

Monster of Mount Rosa, Switzerland

More than Nine Feet Long and as Thick as a Giant Tree, Yellow-Green in Color. Dozens of people in Mount Rosa, Switzerland, have claimed that they have seen a monster in recent days. It looks like a dragon. This creature has lived in the nearby dense forest for four years and has been glimpsed from time to time. It has only recently hidden. According to an eyewitness, the creature is actually a giant python, yellow-green in color, more than nine feet long, and as thick as a giant tree. The farmers in the nearby village are extremely frightened. The authorities are now organizing a large team to capture this monster so that the villagers will not tremble when they go out at night. (Yulin Daily, Special Dispatch, August 14th)

Continuing Reports on the Italian Floods

The scene in the vicinity of Milan and Ovada today is bleak. Yesterday's heavy rain has turned the plains into lakes. Many people and animals have drowned, and the loss of property is immeasurable. The villages of Marassi and Capriata are almost completely destroyed. In Ovada, over 130 houses have been washed away. Rescue efforts are continuing around the clock, but are hampered by muddy terrain and continuing rainfall. It is therefore difficult to ascertain the number of casualties in the coming days. Excessive rainfall from Monday night to Tuesday morning caused the water level in Lake Bassignana to rise sharply, from 5 million cubic meters to 15 million cubic meters. Finally, a 200-meter embankment collapsed with a loud crash. Because the lake level was higher than the surrounding plains, the floodwaters were extremely powerful, sweeping away everything in their path. The disaster area is 40 kilometers long and 2 kilometers wide. (14th National Dispatch)

According to a report from the committee sent to the Morèl area near Milan to investigate the cause of the lake gate collapse, the collapse was due to continuous heavy rain that raised the lake's water level 15 feet higher than normal, putting excessive pressure on the stone foundation. However, the lake's main water gate, built solidly, was not damaged. Only the nearby reservoir, used for power generation, could not withstand the pressure and collapsed first. Then, the torrent rushed into the lake below, and the lake gate was finally washed away, emptying the reservoir completely. As a result, the lake's water volume, which usually holds 18 million cubic meters, is now only 2 million cubic meters. Although the rain has not stopped, there is no longer a risk of the lake gate collapsing again. This lake and its power generation equipment were built ten years ago, and this is the first time the water gate has collapsed. The investigation committee has been ordered to study methods for repairs. (15th National Dispatch)

"Liaozhai" Translated into German

(Reuters, Berlin, July 23) Mr. Peng, a Chinese lecturer at the University of Breslau, has translated 38 stories from *Liaozhai Zhiyi* into German. The translation has now been published. According to Mr. Peng, he devoted great effort to translating this book, striving to accurately convey the original meaning.

Japanese Army Discusses Nagata Incident: A Truly Regrettable Matter for Military Reputation; Serious Impact on Tiger's Aftermath; Current Important Task within the Control Department

(Nanjing) After the cabinet meeting on the 15th, Army Minister Hayashi met with the press corps and initially expressed his feelings regarding the assassination of Military Affairs Bureau Chief Nagata. Here is a transcript of his remarks: "Lieutenant General Nagata's sudden death on the 12th of this month is truly regrettable for the reputation of the national army. I am deeply responsible, feeling that my lack of virtue has led to this. Regarding this incident, appropriate follow-up measures must be taken to establish control within the department going forward. I feel this is my major responsibility at present. However, this is an unprecedented major case for the army, and its impact is very serious. We must pay close attention to it. The details of the crime are currently being investigated by a court-martial and are not yet suitable for discussion. As for the follow-up measures, I did not make any statements on the cabinet floor today, but I am considering appropriate measures. Prime Minister Okada also said that he would do his best to find a solution and expressed hopes for a proper resolution and offered words of encouragement." (15th Japan United Press)

Japanese Cabinet Decides: Crackdown on Strange Documents; Will Be Made into Law and Strictly Enforced; Army Minister Hayashi Visits Prime Minister Okada Yesterday

(Tokyo) When Army Minister Hayashi explained the reasons for the assassination of Bureau Chief Nagata at the cabinet meeting on the 15th, he said, "Blindly following the contents of strange documents" led to this unfortunate incident. These strange documents were clearly the cause of the incident. Therefore, as a result of repeated discussions, the cabinet decided that the crackdown on these strange documents must be strictly enforced. It was agreed that relevant ministries, such as the Ministry of Interior and the Ministry of Justice, would study the matter in detail and then submit it as a bill to the next session of the Diet. It is also reported that those who issue these strange documents will be subject to substantial penalties, and enforcement will be strict. (15th Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi visited Prime Minister Okada at 9:30 AM on the 15th to report on the details of the assassination of Major General Nagata and the interrogation of Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa, the perpetrator. He then explained his determination, saying that the assassination of the Military Affairs Bureau Chief was extremely regrettable for the control of the military. He felt greatly responsible. However, due to the seriousness of the situation, he did not want to be constrained by the issue of responsibility and was determined to actively implement follow-up measures to rectify military discipline in order to strengthen the control of the military. Once all goals have been achieved and the incident resolved, he would take full responsibility and decide on his future course. Prime Minister Okada replied that the cabinet unanimously hoped that the Army Minister would remain in his position and encouraged him to advance the goal of controlling the national army. (15th Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi explained the assassination of Major General Nagata and his policy on controlling the military at the cabinet meeting on the 14th. After the meeting, he immediately summoned Vice-Minister Hashimoto and Military Affairs Bureau Chief Imai to his official residence to discuss how to control the military. According to Army Minister Hayashi's opinion, a perfunctory formal instruction would be ineffective. Therefore, he ordered Vice-Minister Hashimoto to study the most effective concrete methods for controlling the military as soon as possible. After receiving the order, Hashimoto immediately discussed concrete methods with Military Affairs Bureau Chief Imai, Chief of the Preparation Bureau Yamaoka, and Chief of the Personnel Bureau Koumiya. It is reported that the content is as follows: (1) Convene a meeting of army commanders and division commanders. (2) Convene a meeting of regimental commanders. (3) Convene a meeting of chiefs of staff. (4) Convey instructions on clearing the military to the three chiefs. However, as the army personnel had not been transferred for long, and because of Nagata's sudden death and Imai's newly appointed position as Military Affairs Bureau Chief, the successor affairs could not be carried out quickly, and various affairs were difficult to handle. Therefore, convening the various meetings mentioned above will take considerable time. Army Minister Hayashi also believes that reforming the upper-level personnel of the military is the most urgent matter for controlling the military, and he plans to express his determination to the other two chiefs within days to implement the reform. (15th Japan United Press)

(Tokyo) Army Minister Hayashi hinted to Prime Minister Okada that he intended to resign after the incident had come to a close. As a result, all parties are paying close attention. Although Prime Minister Okada and the cabinet members earnestly requested that Army Minister Hayashi remain in his position, Army Minister Hayashi's intention to resign is firm. Therefore, his resignation may be a matter of time. (15th Den-tsu Dispatch)

(Tokyo) It is rumored that Army Minister Hayashi expressed his intention to resign at the meeting of the three chiefs, so his resignation has most likely become a matter of time. However, the special army commander and division commander meeting for the initial handling of this incident will be held at the end of August, so he is unlikely to submit his resignation this month. As for the successor to the Army Minister, it is planned that General Watanabe, the Director-General of Military Education, will succeed him. It is also planned to have Military Councilor General Kawashima or General Abe Nobuyuki succeed as Director-General of Military Education. If the two generals decline, General Terauchi, commander of the Taiwan Army, will be recommended. (15th Den-tsu Dispatch)

British and French First Agree on the Principles of the Tripartite Conference; Based on the 1929 Exchange of Notes between Britain and Italy; As the Basis for Negotiations on the Italian-Abyssinian Question

(Paris) According to reliable sources, British cabinet minister Eden has agreed with French Prime Minister Laval on the key points of the tripartite conference on the Abyssinian issue, namely: (1) Handling the Italian-Abyssinian dispute purely within the framework of the League of Nations. (2) France will not interfere in the negotiations between Britain and Italy. During the talks, both expressed deep concern about maintaining peace and fulfilling the obligations of the League of Nations, and both believed that the tripartite conference could provide a final opportunity to reach a peaceful solution before the League of Nations' meeting on September 4. Eden clearly stated at the time that if war broke out in Africa, it would inevitably lead to broader events in Europe and elsewhere. British public opinion on the issue of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute can be said to be consistent.

The French government has learned of Britain's plan to grant Italy economic concessions in Abyssinia. The content of this plan has not yet been disclosed, but it is said to be consistent with (1) the 1906 treaty guaranteeing the territorial integrity of Abyssinia and delineating the spheres of influence of the three countries, and (2) the 1928 Italian-Abyssinian treaty and the League of Nations Covenant. In 1925, Britain and Italy exchanged notes in which Italy recognized Britain's right to dispose of Lake Tana, and Britain did not object to Italy's plan to build railways in the hinterland of Eritrea and Italian Somaliland. This document can now serve as the basis for negotiations. What is necessary is to persuade Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to accept the rights granted by Britain and France to Italy to develop colonial enterprises. It is now expected that Britain and France will use their influence to persuade the Abyssinian Emperor to grant these rights to Italy. At yesterday's talks, Laval was assisted by the political director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Bargeton, while Eden was assisted by the Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Sir Vansittart.

Italian representative Baron Aloisi is expected to arrive in Paris today and will meet with the French Prime Minister. Representatives from France, Britain, and Italy will begin formal talks on Friday as scheduled. Last night, Laval held talks with the Greek Minister to Paris, Politis. Politis has been appointed as the fifth arbitrator of the arbitration committee for the Walwal incident. The committee had previously been suspended due to differences of opinion between the parties and is now resuming its work. (15th Reuters)

Italian Representative Arrives in Paris: Will Meet with Laval Immediately

(Paris) Italian representative Aloisi, along with his entourage, arrived here from Italy at 9:35 AM today to participate in the tripartite conference between Britain, France, and Italy. Aloisi then went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 11:00 AM to meet with French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval, and the talks ended at 12:20 PM. (15th Havas)

(Paris) Italian chief representative Aloisi arrived here this morning and immediately went to meet with French Prime Minister Laval for an hour and fifteen minutes. No one else was present at the time. The content of the talks is unknown. The French Prime Minister later told reporters that the tripartite conference would begin tomorrow, and Laval would meet with British representative Eden again this afternoon. (15th Reuters)

(Paris) According to sources from Havas, Italian representative Aloisi vigorously defended Italy's position during his talks with Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval this morning, saying that Italy, due to its increasing population, cannot accommodate it within its own borders, so it must obtain political privileges in Abyssinia. Furthermore, to defend Italian Somaliland and Eritrea, it is also necessary to obtain such political privileges. Merely obtaining economic privileges is not sufficient. Italy has now sent 170,000 troops to concentrate in its East African territories. If a satisfactory peaceful solution cannot be obtained, it is prepared to intervene militarily at any time. As for the scope of Italy's demands for resolving the dispute, it will only be put forward after the tripartite conference opens tomorrow. Furthermore, Italy mobilized another 50,000 troops yesterday. Italy is determined to uphold its original position, which can be seen here. Laval will now report Aloisi's statement to British Minister without Portfolio Eden this afternoon. Italy has indicated that it must obtain political privileges, while Britain opposes political concessions. The positions of the two countries are clearly divergent. It is generally believed that Laval will reconcile the views of Britain and Italy and find a compromise solution, advocating a peaceful resolution to the Italian-Abyssinian dispute and granting Italy substantial benefits. (15th Havas)

(Rome) The semi-official "Foreign Affairs Report" commented on the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, saying, "Giving Abyssinia an outlet to the Red Sea, restricting Abyssinia's economic concessions, and entrusting the League of Nations with governance are all means to disguise Britain's trusteeship in Abyssinia. To reach a compromise resolution of the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, it is necessary to abandon the above methods." The report also said that while Italy recognizes the treaty-based rights of Britain, Italy is unwilling to use Italian blood as the price of expanding the British Empire. The report then enumerated various actions by Britain that lack friendship towards Italy, such as inciting Abyssinia to mobilize its troops, threatening to block the Suez Canal, and increasing the garrison troops in British territories near Abyssinia. The report said, "The reason why Britain does not want Italy's power to penetrate Abyssinia is that if there is an opportunity, Britain will engulf Abyssinia and occupy it. Britain intends to impoverish Italy, so that the raw materials needed by Italy will have to rely on the British Empire. However, Italy is not afraid of this threat. Recalling 105 years ago, when France launched an expedition to Algiers in Africa, Britain also made similar incitements, which shows that this is Britain's habitual trick, so what should we fear?" (14th Havas)

There are a total of 499,682 Jews in Germany, of which about 4% of Berlin's total population reside in Berlin. Details of Beijing's Prostitution Rescue Measures

(Nanjing) The Women's Association drafted the following measures for rescuing prostitutes: 1. Women under the age of 17 and those who are pregnant shall not be forced into prostitution. 2. Prostitutes' residences should be designated to specific areas and should not be mixed with respectable women's residences. 3. Special regulations should be made for the prostitutes' clothing to avoid confusion. 4. Guidance should be provided for them to learn a trade, with a limit of three months. If they refuse guidance after the deadline, they will be sent to the municipal relief home for training. 5. Brothel keepers shall not be allowed to mistreat them. However, whether the Social Affairs Bureau will immediately lift the ban on prostitution is still under discussion. (15th Special Dispatch)

Public Telegram

Telegram from Tongling County, Anhui, Requesting Relief - To the Shanghai Shen Bao Newspaper Office: The people of Tongling have been afflicted by Heaven and are now suffering from floods. This summer, the upper reaches of the Yangtze River experienced torrential floods, and all the counties along the river in our Anhui have suffered. Tongling County has always been known as having "three mountains and seven weirs." The dikes of all sizes throughout the county are arranged like scales. Since (month omitted), officials and civilians have been guarding them day and night, sparing no effort. However, the water level increased day by day, and with the intrusion of strong winds, more than fifty large and small dikes eventually collapsed, inundating over 90,000 mu of land and causing approximately 800,000 yuan in agricultural losses. More than 8,000 households, totaling over 40,000 people, were affected, accounting for an estimated one-quarter of the county's population. 5,000 houses were destroyed, and countless livestock and farming tools were lost. People are scattered and displaced, eating in the wind and sleeping in the dew, their cries and lamentations unbearable to hear. Autumn is approaching, and our sorrow deepens. In the past, when the weirs and villages suffered disasters, they could still seek food in the mountain villages. But now, the mountain villages have not yet recovered from the severe drought of the previous year and cannot even take care of themselves. Moreover, there has been no rain for forty days, and a drought is looming, which is even more worrying. Therefore, although the water level may be lower than in the twentieth year of the Republic, the disaster is actually more severe. The county magistrate and others are heartbroken and are urgently seeking relief. In addition to establishing a disaster relief committee to actively handle relief work, we have prepared tables listing the affected weirs and respectfully request relief. We specially request your newspaper to appeal on our behalf so that charitable organizations and generous benefactors can provide aid and food to save the disaster-stricken people. We are filled with anticipation. Attached is a table (omitted). With respectful regards, the Tongling County Government, County Party Headquarters, People's Food Regulation Committee Branch, Finance Committee, Chambers of Commerce, Farmers' Associations, Educational Associations, Changpingcang Granary General Branch and various branches, Education Bureau, District Public Offices, all respectfully kowtow and stamp.

A Record of Inspecting Flood Conditions Along the Rivers - A Glimpse of the Disaster Along the Pinghan Railway

The steamer from Tianmen to Hankou departed at 3:00 AM. Passing by the Diaochahu Lake, bays intertwined, and reeds grew densely. It was once the nest of the Red area in central Hubei. Tianmen's four townships were also deeply infiltrated by communism in the past. Since its recovery three years ago, the local authorities have worked hard on construction and have earned a reputation as a model county. Unexpectedly, the god of the river caused trouble, and everything was swept away again. Such a huge change in fortune! In a country where human power cannot control nature, the consequences are unpredictable. Leaving the lake and entering the river channel, the villages on the shore that have not been washed away are already inhabited by returning disaster victims. Some are transporting bricks and shoveling mud to repair broken houses (the majority), while others are sunning and threshing spoiled wheat, hoping to satisfy their hunger with the remaining grains. Survivors of the disaster all wear sad expressions. Hawks and crows, looking around at the vast expanse of water, have all become waterfowl. I could only fly along the embankment to find special food, my beak dripping with muddy blood, I couldn't bear to think about what I was eating. I arrived in Hankou at dusk. The green willows and tall buildings on both sides of the river were bathed in the afterglow of the setting sun. The scenery was beautiful, and the men and women were enjoying the cool air, as if there was no sound of the Jianghan River converging and surging, which slightly moved people's hearts. I am afraid that those who are intoxicated by the leisurely life of brocade clothes and jade food in the city will no longer remember that there are still thousands upon thousands of starving disaster victims in the world. As the ship docked, before the passengers could disembark, more than a dozen male and female disaster victims rushed forward and squeezed their way onto the ship, eager to board. The ship police stopped them and asked, "Where are you going?" They replied sadly, "We want to go downstream (referring to various places downstream) to escape the disaster." The ship police continued, "There are also floods in the next few provinces. Where is a good place to go? Besides, this is a ship specifically for Tianmen, not a ship going down the Yangtze River." One person pleaded, "We also just escaped from Tianmen two days ago. We sat by the river for two days, and no one took us in. One of our companions went to beg for food and disappeared. The rest of us are afraid of getting lost and dare not leave. We are so hungry that we have to sell our clothes for two or eight hundred coins to buy rice to cook porridge. We really can't stand the hunger anymore, so we want to escape to a better place in the next few provinces. Please do a good deed." The ship police shouted angrily, "The ship is not doing good deeds. Get out of here!" A passenger interjected, "Why don't you (referring to the disaster victims) pull rickshaws?" Immediately, a rickshaw puller who was hustling for business replied, "Brother, I have been in Hankou for three or four years, and I am still not familiar with the streets of the concession. Newcomers from the countryside want to pull rickshaws? Humph, that's easy!" In addition, there were those who suggested registering with the Hubei Flood Relief Association, and those who advised them to beg for alms from various charitable organizations. The discussions were chaotic and resembled drawing cakes to satisfy hunger, and ultimately did not provide any practical help to the displaced disaster victims.

That night, I took the Pinghan train north. Near the Dazhimen station, no less than hundreds of residents were sleeping naked under the shade of the trees. The area was full of accumulated water and weeds, which easily bred flies and mosquitoes. Sleeping in the open air was certainly cool, but ultimately not conducive to hygiene. But compared to the disaster victims huddled together on the banks of the (omitted) water, exposed to the sun and steam during the day and fearing the arrival of storms again at night, these people were no less than resting in a peaceful paradise. A Mr. Wang from Huangpi in the seat, told of the flood in his county, saying, "On the seventh day of July, suddenly there was a strong wind and rain, and the rice seedlings by the lake were completely submerged. The Xiang River also suddenly rose sharply, rushing and surging, and successively washed away the Minsheng Sanyang and other (omitted) dikes. More than 100,000 mu of farmland in the southwest of the county town were inundated, and 150,000 to 60,000 people were affected. Some lived on the hills, exposed to the wind and dew, while others clung to the rooftops, shaken by the waves. Others gathered in the county town, overflowing the streets. Everyone was emaciated and covered in mud, in a terrible state. The men cried and the women wailed, which was unbearable to hear. Recently, as the water has gradually receded, the higher ground can be replanted with buckwheat, but the low-lying areas will likely be difficult to replant. If the soil is sandy, radishes and sweet potatoes can be planted, but seeds and fertilizer are a problem everywhere. I urgently hope that agricultural relief will arrive in time, or there may be a glimmer of hope."

At midnight, I arrived in Xiaogan. Disaster victims who had been waiting for a long time, supporting the old and carrying the young, swarmed into the military car. Although there were road police outside scolding and soldiers inside rejecting them, (omitted) the disaster victims struggled for their last chance of survival. Relying on the strength of the crowd, they used all kinds of methods, both soft and hard, and finally achieved the goal of riding the train for free without paying a fare. They were also fortunate enough to be among the soldiers who had previously wanted to reject them (soldiers also do not buy tickets for slow trains). It can also be said that there was a lot of luck. According to the first, second, and third districts of Xiaogan, which are located in the low-lying areas in the south, at the intersection of the Huanshui and Yunshui rivers, the water outlet for (omitted) the counties of Yunmeng, Yingcheng, and Tianmen. Wherever the lakes and streams reached, everything became a swamp. The Phoenix Terrace, one of the so-called eight scenic spots in Xiaogan, was built during the Xianfeng period of the Qing Dynasty. It towers into the clouds and has never been submerged, but this time the water level even reached the steps. The loss of fields, houses, livestock, and people in low-lying areas was naturally unavoidable. In addition, the stele of "The Hometown of Dong Yong, the Filial Piety of the Han Dynasty" is still intact outside the city. The disaster victims seemed to value historical sites more than their lives, so they praised it endlessly.

The next morning, passing through Wusheng Pass, the mountain was cut open and a tunnel was built, which is the first large mountain passed by the Pinghan Railway. The south of the tunnel is the territory of Yingshan County, Hubei, and the north of the tunnel is the territory of Xinyang County, Henan. In the past, the north and south were (omitted) governed separately, and this was once the boundary. Next to it is the Drumming Terrace. During the Spring and Autumn Period, King Zhuang of Chu refused to fight Yue Jiao and personally beat the drums here, hence the name. About ten miles north is the Xindian Station. Fourteen miles east of the station is Jigong Mountain, with towering peaks and verdant clouds and mist. Westerners have built many buildings on the top of the mountain in the name of the church, making it a summer resort comparable to Lushan Mountain. To the west of the station, there are giant rocks of fifty or sixty feet, scattered on the ridge in a soaring posture, hence the name Longpao Mountain (Dragon Running Mountain). It is said that there is still a fairy's boot in the belly of the mountain, a stone boot shape, ingeniously made by nature. At the foot of the mountain there is a stone drum, which makes a loud sound when struck. From here, the trees are shady, the fragrant grass covers the ground, and the red beans and yellow millet are especially beautiful and lovely.

The train passed through Xinyang and stopped for a long time. The county is the cultural and commercial center of southern Henan. Although mountain floods have erupted, it has not suffered from floods due to its superior terrain. Exports include grains, cotton, cowhide, bamboo ware, and chicken and duck eggs. For middle and high school education, there is one provincial senior normal school and one county junior middle school. The authorities of each school, in view of the fact that the four townships and neighboring areas of the county had been reduced to communist areas in the past, take an interventionist approach to extracurricular activities and a strict approach to all regular courses in order to prevent students from becoming radical in their thinking. Smoking is also prohibited on weekdays, and violators are severely punished. However, if teachers and staff do not lead by example, I am afraid that the results may not be satisfactory. In the city there is a tower called Chaoyang Tower, more than ten feet high, built during the Zhengde period of the Ming Dynasty. There is a well under the tower, which is rare in other places. A few miles west of the station is the Zigong Temple, with the words "The Former Sage Zigong was the Minister here" inscribed on the stele.

The train passed Queshan and arrived at Zhumadian, which is very prosperous in commerce and is a distribution center for goods in the vicinity. More than ten miles east of the station, the mountains are rugged, and there is a so-called ancient city. It is said that this is where Guan Yu beheaded Cai Yang. Cai Yang's tomb is still there today. There is a Zhang Mingfu Temple in the city, dedicated to Zhang Xi of the Eastern Han Dynasty. Xi was the magistrate of Pingyu in Caizhou. There was a great drought and he prayed for rain but it did not come. He burned himself with firewood, and then the sky rained heavily. The people were grateful for his virtue and built a temple to worship him. Although Xi's self-immolation was close to superstition, he was still a worthy official on the historical record. However, since Dayu's water control, which achieved great achievements, the history of disasters for thousands of years has been almost entirely a record of droughts and floods. Especially in this era of scientific advancement, water conservancy agencies in various places are springing up like mushrooms after rain, and spending increases every year to prevent floods and droughts, but droughts and floods still occur every year. The competent authorities are responsible and cannot shirk their responsibility. I don't know how they can justify themselves. A robbery occurred at the Xindian Station a month ago. First, bandits disguised themselves as passengers, bought tickets and entered the station. When the train arrived at the station, they each took out small pistols hidden in their sleeves, and divided up the key points of each car. The road police were caught off guard and could not respond, and eleven rifles were taken away. Fortunately, no other passengers were injured or lost property. Now, the Xinyang to Juan City section has been assigned additional road police to strictly prevent and control the situation, and there is no danger. Juan City has fertile soil and is all plains. This time, due to the floods of the Shahe and Luohe rivers, many fields and crops were submerged. As the train entered the county, there was standing water everywhere, and the roots of the crops were still submerged in the water by several inches. Those that were damaged by the rushing torrents have also been replanted with buckwheat where the water has receded. Fortunately, the county seat was not flooded, and only a few people and animals in the four townships were lost. However, there was a great loss of grain. Traveling north from Juan City, passing through Meng Temple Village to Xiaoshang Bridge, the roadbed of the railway had been washed away for more than 20 miles. In one section, about four miles long, the entire roadbed was washed away, and the rails were empty, like a bridge. Half a month ago, train traffic was blocked because of this. It has now been repaired with extra effort, but the roadbed has been filled and the stone ballast has not been laid, so the train runs slowly and softly. After passing this section, it speeds up again as before.

Commerce and education in Juan City are no less developed than in Xinyang in southern Henan. The Luowan River Town, about a mile southeast of the city, is crowded with boats, and hundreds of merchants gather, making it more prosperous than the county seat. The main exports are sesame, soybeans, cowhide, and paulownia wood. In the past, paulownia wood was sold exclusively to Japan, but in recent years it has declined. Primary and secondary schools in the city are well-developed, but the four townships are very conservative, and the custom of foot binding has not yet been completely changed. There is a Gui Village Town in the eastern township, which is where Confucius thought of returning while in Chen. Outside the east gate there is also a stele erected during the Qing Dynasty commemorating Confucius's thoughts of returning.

Fujian Province - Relief for Floods and Plague - Wind and Rain Cause Disasters in Southern and Eastern Fujian - Plague Discovered in Northern and Western Fujian

Fuzhou News, This time, due to wind and rain, the counties of Putian, Xianyou, Hui'an, Jinjiang, Nan'an, Yongchun, Tong'an, Anxi, Longxi in Southern Fujian, and Lianjiang and Nanri in Eastern Fujian, suffered disasters. People and livestock were swept away, houses collapsed, fields and crops were destroyed, trees were broken, roads were damaged, and countless bridges were destroyed. The provincial government has received reports from various counties every day. In total, no less than 100,000 people have been affected, and the losses are estimated at over 10 million yuan. The severity of the disaster and the extent of the affected area are unprecedented in recent decades. In terms of roads, the Construction Department has instructed the Putian-Hua'an, Quanzhou, and Zhangzhou Highway Engineering Offices to repair the roads in sections as quickly as possible, which is expected to take two weeks. In addition to the cost of labor and materials, which will require more than 200,000 yuan, the Chairman of the Provincial Government, Chen Yi, convened the Chairman of the Relief Committee, Chen Peikun, the Director of the Civil Affairs Department, Gao Dengting, and others to discuss relief measures. It was decided that the various counties should quickly investigate and report the actual situation of the disaster. The Civil Affairs Department should send two inspectors, He Jing and Chen Huanglin, to the various counties in Southern and Eastern Fujian to conduct on-the-spot investigations of the disaster situation, so as to plan relief measures in a coordinated manner. The Relief Committee should first raise 10,000 yuan to handle urgent relief, specifically to help the homeless disaster victims, with 2,000 yuan for Anxi, 1,500 yuan each for Hui'an, Tong'an, Jinjiang, Longxi, and Nan'an, 1,000 yuan for Lianjiang, and 500 yuan for Nanri. It will then report to the Central Relief Committee and request the allocation of a large sum of money for relief. The report stated, "Since the end of last month, Fujian Province has experienced two hurricanes and rainstorms. It only calmed down slightly on Geng day. According to reports from the Fourth and Fifth District Administrative Commissioners and the county magistrates of Hui'an, Anxi, Longxi, Jinjiang, Lianjiang, Nan'an, and other counties, after the wind disaster, there was a mountain flood with water over ten feet high, and the cities became swamps. People, livestock, food, and houses were swept away, and the disaster was extremely severe, unprecedented in decades. Telephone lines were damaged, ships were grounded, roads were washed away, and all transportation was cut off. The disaster situation in the coastal counties has not yet been fully reported, and it may be even more tragic. We have sent personnel to take detours to investigate and are planning to provide urgent relief. However, Fujian Province has suffered from banditry for many years, and the people are already deeply impoverished. Although it has been gradually settled, the wounds have not healed and vitality is depleted. They have suffered another partial disaster, how can the people bear it? The only thing to do is to quickly allocate a large sum of relief money to Fujian for relief and to ease their suffering. According to investigations, this flood occurred during the fruiting and ripening season of late rice and seasonal fruits, all of which were swept away by the typhoon. The farmers suffered the greatest losses, and their livelihoods in the second half of the year will be affected." In addition, a plague broke out in Yanping in Northern Fujian and Longyan in Western Fujian a month ago. In Northern Fujian, after the government and social organizations jointly established an epidemic prevention association to help treat the disease, the epidemic situation has gradually subsided in recent days. However, in Western Fujian, due to the major battles last year, corpses were scattered everywhere and many were not collected, causing the atmosphere to become increasingly severe, and the number of deaths increased daily. The provincial government has ordered all medical teams in Western Fujian to concentrate in Longyan to help treat the disease. It also telegraphed the Ministry of Health to send experts to Fujian to preside over the epidemic prevention efforts as soon as possible. Yesterday, the ministry sent Yang Yongnian, a technician from the ministry and director of the inspection institute of the Health Department of the Economic Commission, along with medical officers Lin Jiarui, He Zhiguang, and Wang Deying, carrying a large amount of medicine, to Fujian from Shanghai. They met with Chairman Chen, stated the epidemic prevention policy, and scheduled to take a boat to Xiamen on the 15th, then transfer to Western Fujian to engage in epidemic prevention work. The provincial government also telegraphed the Zhangzhou Pacification Command to assist in the progress after Yang arrives. (August 14th)

Guangdong Province - Remaining Bandits in the Eastern District Eliminated - Time Limit for All Counties to Organize Baojia - Reorganization of Regular and Reserve Police Forces

Guangzhou Communication, In recent days, Guangdong Province has vigorously implemented the Baojia system, conducted household registration in various villages, and reported bandits, so that bandits have nowhere to hide. At the same time, four Pacification Commands were established in the northwest, southeast, and central regions to carry out Pacification work. In the eastern district, because a few bandits from the Kun, Lian, and Jiangxi borders and the Fujian border fled to Phoenix Mountain in Raoping and Nanshan at the junction of Jieyang and Chaoyang, the defense forces of the eastern district have repeatedly sent teams to search and suppress them. It has now been found that a group near Raoping, after being surrounded and suppressed by Zeng Youren's Brigade of the First Independent Division under Huang Renhuan, captured more than 40 bandits and seized more than 100 rifles. They have recently been eliminated one by one. As for the bandits in Nanshan, the Ninth Division has also dispatched teams to search for them separately. Communist Party fake organizations such as the Dongjiang Special Committee, the County Soviet, and repair shops, grain bureaus, and post offices have all been destroyed. The bandit leader Gu Dacun has now fled, and more than 30 other notorious bandits, including Yuan Xinyun, Lai Yuheng, Xie Ronghua, Zeng Jiuhua, and Lin Sanji, have surrendered. Among those captured were Tao Yao, Chen Gengguang, He Fusheng, Xu Zigui, Tian Leguang, and the female bandit Wu Yingdi, totaling more than 70 people. Those killed included the female bandit Zeng Yulian and the bandit leaders Zhang Mukui, Gu Hanming, and Luo Pinghan. The Eastern District Pacification Command has now sent letters to the governments of all counties, setting a deadline of the end of August for the completion of the Baojia organization in each county. The steps for handling this are roughly divided into three items: (1) The county should immediately appoint personnel to supervise the district and township chiefs in the county to complete the Baojia organization before the end of August in accordance with the Baojia Regulations. (2) If district and township chiefs or people in the district delay or deliberately resist the organization of Baojia, they should be strictly investigated. (3) After the Baojia is organized in each county and district, the roster should be submitted to the government in charge for future reference, so that personnel can be sent to conduct random checks. As for the district and township guard teams, they have also been reorganized recently. If the captains of the regular guard teams in each middle and small team are deemed to have insufficient knowledge and are unqualified, they should be trained or replaced immediately. If the soldiers in the regular team are all of foreign nationality, efforts should be made to gradually promote the conscription system. The soldiers should be trained in rotation. As for the reserve team, the training in academic subjects should follow balanced instruction and should not focus on technical subjects, etc.

Songjiang - The Reaction to the Brokerage Fee Demands of the Firewood Guild

The residents of Songjiang County use rice straw and chaff as fuel. Farmers in the suburbs often carry firewood to sell, while farmers from further away transport it by boat to the urban area for sale. There are also people from Jiangbei who transport and sell it. However, the firewood guilds, relying on having a license from the Finance Department, would detain firewood boats and demand brokerage fees. The farmers could not bear this harassment. The County Chamber of Commerce discussed this at the 24th Executive Committee meeting, stating that there is a difference between farmers selling firewood and chaff and those who specialize in selling it. How can they be forced to pay brokerage fees, disrupting tranquility? It was decided to submit a request to the County Government to instruct the Public Security Bureau to send police to suppress this practice in order to provide relief.

Suzhou - Old Man Sentenced for Rape of Young Girl

The case of Wang Renchang, a 67-year-old man, raping Han Xingbao, a 13-year-old girl, has been investigated by the Public Security Bureau and handed over to the local court for trial. The trial has now concluded and the verdict was delivered yesterday. Wang Renchang was sentenced to three years imprisonment. Wang Renchang refused to accept the verdict and attempted suicide in court. The bailiffs took Wang away and sent him back to the detention center.

Wuxi - Xinxin Fire Causes Tens of Thousands in Losses

Yesterday (15th) morning at 6:00 AM, a fire broke out due to an electrical fault on the second-story loft of the Xinxin Silk Store on North Main Street. The fire spread to the floor below. Fortunately, the store had its own pump and water tank and immediately used fire hydrants to extinguish the fire. By the time the various fire brigades arrived to help extinguish the fire, the fire had already been brought under control. As a result, four rooms on the loft floor had their roofs burned through. Including the water damage, the losses were estimated at 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. Fortunately, the store had fire insurance worth 70,000 yuan from Baolong, Shenchang, Huanqiu, and other companies, so the losses were not too great. Yesterday, the store sorted out the goods and was temporarily closed for one day. It will reopen as usual today.

Visiting Relatives and Being Humiliated Leads to Hanging Suicide

Zhu Liu, a woman from Cangqiao Township, Yanqiao Town, Fifth District, was over 50 years old. She had three sons and one daughter. Her daughter, Rongxiu, was married to Gao A'shi, a resident of Gaojiaqiao. However, A'shi's mother, Gao, was quite fierce and often scolded Rongxiu. Rongxiu told her mother, Zhu Liu, about the abuse. Zhu went to negotiate, which started with an argument and then turned into a physical fight. As a result, both sides were injured. After being persuaded by neighbors, the conflict subsided. However, after Liu returned home, she became overwhelmed with anger and conceived a hatred for the world. She hanged herself the day before yesterday. The Fifth District Tutu Zheng, Zhou Longhui, reported this to the court for investigation. Yesterday (15th) morning at 8:00 AM, the acting prosecutor went to the countryside to conduct an autopsy. It was determined that she had committed suicide by hanging. It was ordered that the corpse's family prepare a coffin for burial, pending further investigation.

Wujin Second-Hand Clothing Stores Forced to Pay Brokerage Fees

The Wujin County Chamber of Commerce has been negotiating with the Wujin Pawn Industry and the Fengji Second-Hand Clothing Store. Yesterday, it sent a telegram to the Provincial Government, the Department of Finance, and the Department of Construction, stating that the nature of a brokerage is to act as an agent for buying and selling, which refers to customers from outside the area, not to those who are already established in the area. It also implies that the brokerage guarantees outside customers for local businesses, so the commission is a matter of rights and obligations. If pawnshops sell goods that have been fully redeemed to clothing stores, both parties are already established businesses and should be free to buy and sell. Why should the brokerage force them to pay? This is obviously disrupting commerce. We dare to send a telegram to ask for your review and verification, to quickly order a strict prohibition to ensure the safety of the commercial market and to prevent others from following suit.

Jiaxing: The Truth About the Disappearance of the Proprietor of a Business Going East

Zhang Wenxin (17 years old), son of Zhang Guangfeng, proprietor of Litong Fengji Carriage Company at Chunbo Bridge, Jiaxing, went out on the morning of the 11th to collect carriage rentals and then disappeared. Guangfeng searched everywhere, but his whereabouts were unknown. At noon, a blackmail letter signed "Gao Xiaoguai" arrived, demanding 500 yuan. After reporting to the river and land police corps for investigation, river and land police officers arrested Xu Tingzhang's son Xu Demao, and Zhang Dingtong, who often associated with Wenxin, for questioning. Later, Xu Tingzhang (a Yancheng native who raises ducks) was arrested and interrogated. It was then learned that Zhang Wenxin was waiting at Xucun Station. An officer from the First Public Security Bureau took police officers on the 14th to bring Zhang Wenxin back for questioning. It was then learned that Wenxin's departure was masterminded by Xu Demao (because Zhang Wenxin had been beaten by his father a few days earlier). Wenxin's erhu (Chinese violin), a pair of leather shoes, and a 500-foot flashlight were also found in Xu's residence. The handwriting of the blackmail letter also resembled Xu Demao's. Therefore, the case has now become clear: it was entirely instigated by Xu Demao alone, and Zhang Dingtong seemed to have little involvement. Currently, the county government believes that because there is a blackmail letter in the case, all the witnesses must be sent to the court for interrogation.

Nantong: Morphia Den Cracked in the North of the City

A morphia-selling den was located at No. 16, Zhao Cheng North City Foot. It was cracked by the Chengqu Public Security Bureau. The seller, Xu Guangyuan, was arrested along with the evidence and transferred to the Main Bureau, which in turn transferred him to the Fourth District Security Command for military trial.

Jinsha: Unclear Cause of Death of a Young Woman

Gu Buou of Jinsha engaged Zhang Shuizhen as his wife. The wedding date was set, but Zhang suddenly died under unclear circumstances. After Gu inquired, he learned that his fiancée had been having an affair with his nephew, Zhang Zuyin, and had an abortion before the wedding, which led to her death. He sued the court. The prosecutor's office sent police to Jinsha to transport Zhang Shuizhen's coffin to the city for an exhumation and autopsy.

Xiaoshan: Bumper Harvest of New Grain, Rice Prices Plunge

Farmers in the fourth district of Xiaoshan planted early rice everywhere. This summer, the weather was favorable, with adequate sunshine and rain, and the crops were not damaged by wind and rain during the flowering season. As a result, the grains are plump and the panicles are especially long. During the harvest a few days ago, each mu (unit of area) yielded three shi (unit of volume) of unhusked rice. The abundance of the harvest is rarely seen in previous years. Farmers are all overjoyed. Furthermore, rice shops in Linpu saw new grain from Zhuji and the local area entering the market due to the bumper harvest. Currently, the supply of goods is surging, and the price of rice has been reduced by 1.5 yuan. New rice is priced at 6.8 yuan per shi, and old rice is sold at 7.4 yuan per shi, a decrease of more than 3 yuan compared to last winter. This is good news for the future of people's food.
