Local News

Shanghai-Wuxi Highway Grand Opening Ceremony Yesterday; Ribbon-cutting in Nanxiang in the Morning, Banquet in Changshu at Noon; Chairman Chen Hosts Guests in Wuxi in the Evening; Long-distance Buses Scheduled to Start Operating on the 17th

The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway, jointly built by the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department and the Shanghai Municipal Government, is 140 kilometers long. Construction began last year in sections and has recently been completed. A grand ribbon-cutting ceremony was held at Guyi Garden in Nanxiang at 8:00 AM on the 15th. Three to four thousand people from Shanghai, Changshu, and Wuxi attended. The Shanghai-Wuxi Motor Company provided vehicles to welcome and transport guests. A banquet was held in Changshu at noon to entertain guests visiting Yushan Mountain and other scenic spots. Chairman Chen hosted a banquet for company directors Zhang Gongquan, Wang Xiaolai, and others at Yiyuan in Wuxi in the evening. The company's passenger buses are scheduled to begin operating on the 17th. The grand opening ceremony and the highway's construction situation are detailed below.

Cars and Dust Non-Stop on the Shanghai-Nanxiang Road

On the morning of the 15th, the weather was clear, and many people from all walks of life in Shanghai went to participate in the ceremony. The Shanghai-Wuxi Motor Company provided 60 public buses for pick-up and drop-off at the intersection of the public road. They started running continuously from 7:00 AM. Many people also went to the meeting in their own cars. For a time, cars and dust were non-stop on the Shanghai-Nanxiang Road. The road is paved with gravel. Although the road surface is narrow, it is as smooth as a whetstone. There is no bumpiness on the road. Small bridges along the way are guarded by military police. Passing through Luyang Town, it enters the territory of Jiading County. There are motor vehicle stations with colorful arches on both sides of the road, with banners hanging in the middle, reading "Welcome Chairman Chen and Director Shen to Jia". Before long, the colorful arch of Guyi Garden came into view. It had arrived in Nanxiang and was the location of the ceremony.

More Than One Thousand Guests Attended

Guyi Garden is a famous garden in Nanxiang with pavilions, bridges, mountains, and water, which is quite secluded and beautiful. The auditorium was set up in the hall behind the garden. In the hall, there was a horizontal plaque written by Dong Qichang, "Hua Yan Mo Hai". The hall was full of national flags. The Party and National flags were hung on the stage. In the middle was a portrait of the Founding Father, and the frame "The Revolution Has Not Yet Succeeded, Comrades Must Continue to Strive." On the table on the stage were two pairs of scissors for the ribbon-cutting, engraved with "Presented by Mayor Wu and Director Shen." The ceremony began at 8:30 AM. Attendees included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director Shen Baixian, Li Shizeng, Huang Boqiao, Pan Gongzhan, Ye Gongchuo, Zhang Gongquan, Yu Zuoting, Yu Qiaqing, Li Zhaohuan, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Liu Zhanen, Wang Yansong, Pan Gengsheng, Mo Heng, Fan Shouzhi, Shen Tianxin, Zheng Yue from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, Zhang Ming, Rong Zongjing, Rong Desheng, Yang Hanxi, Wang Boqi, Xu Shiying, Huang Bodu, Huang Renzhi, Pan Yangyao, Lu Bohong, Wang Manyun, Cheng Shewo, Mao Heyuan, Pan Xulun, Xi Yushu, Xiao Youmei, Liu Haisu, Songhu Garrison Commander Li Duchu, Zhu Tingyu from the Ministry of Navy, Wen Chongxin, Ye Wenzheng from Changshu County Government, Shi Minyong, Cai Degong from the County Party Department, and the Education Bureau, more than one thousand people. The Shanghai Municipal Police Band played music, and a team led by Zhang Shichuan from the Mingxing Film Company, including cinematographer Dong Keyi, arrived at the scene to film along the way.

The Ceremony Began at 8:00 AM

At 8:00 AM, the ceremony began. The Shanghai Municipal Police Band played music to open the meeting. (1) The highest respect was paid to the Party and National flags and the portrait of the Founding Father. (2) Chairman Wu Tiecheng respectfully read the Founding Father's will. (3) Chairman Wu Tiecheng reported. (4) Director Shen reported on the construction process. (5) Wang Xiaolai, director of the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Motor Company, reported. (6) Chen Qicai and Yu Zuoting gave speeches. (7) Music was played. (8) Photography.

Wu Reported on the Preparations

Chairman Wu Tiecheng reported on the preparation of the Shanghai-Wuxi Road. The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway, together with the Suzhou-Changshu branch road, has been completed. Now that the opening ceremony is being held, I would like to briefly report on the preparation process as follows: The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway and the Suzhou-Changshu branch road are important routes for connecting the inland areas of Jiangsu Province and connecting Shanghai and Wuxi. The areas through which it passes include Jiading, Taicang, Changshu, Wuxi, and Wuxian counties, which are all areas rich in products and densely populated. In the past, the travels between Suzhou, Changshu, Taicang, and Jiading, and between Wuxi and Changshu, all relied on waterways. Often, they were separated by dozens of miles, taking more than a day. Transportation was extremely inconvenient. Therefore, the construction of the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway is extremely important. Chairman Chiang was concerned about highway construction and telegraphed in September of the 22nd year of the Republic of China to prepare for the construction of Tan Road and complete it within a time limit. After receiving the order, I invited leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai to initiate the organization of the Shanghai-Wuxi Road Long-Distance Motor Company and first established a preparatory committee, with Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Gongquan, Chen Guangfu, Qian Xinzhi, Guo Hehui, Yang Hanxi, Qian Sunqing, Sun Zhizhai, Rong Zongjing, and myself as preparatory members, and Wang Xiaolai was elected as the director to prepare for all matters related to the construction of the road and the opening of traffic. However, the Shanghai-Wuxi Road is 140 kilometers long, and the Suzhou-Changshu branch road is 39 kilometers long, totaling 179 kilometers. The route is long, and the funding is huge. After actively raising funds, the provincial and municipal governments and the Shanghai-Wuxi Road Long-Distance Motor Company negotiated the road construction plan and signed a contract, granting the company the exclusive right to operate on the two roads. The entire road project was originally scheduled to be completed in May of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Later, due to the impact of the sluggish market on the company, it was not easy to raise share capital, which caused the road construction project to be slightly delayed. However, thanks to the efforts of the shareholders of the company, two loans were borrowed to meet the needs of road construction, and the entire road project was completed today. The efforts of the shareholders and the speed of road construction by the provincial government are admirable. The company was officially established at the end of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Fifteen directors and seven supervisors were elected. Zhang Gongquan was elected as chairman, and Wang Xiaolai and others were elected as standing directors. Wang Xiaolai was hired as the general manager to actively plan the vehicle equipment. After several months of preparation, everything was ready by the end of June of this year. Therefore, the opening ceremony was held today. It is hoped that after the opening of this road, the culture of the various places along the road will progress day by day, and passenger and freight transport will be more convenient. The land transportation between this city and Zhejiang Province, in addition to the railway, already has the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. Now, the Shanghai-Wuxi Highway has been built to connect with the inland areas of Jiangsu Province. In the future, if it can be expanded to complete the highway network of the provinces in the south of the Yangtze River, the prospects are truly unlimited. I am very grateful that the provincial and municipal governments and leaders from all walks of life have come to participate in the meeting. I will briefly report the situation of the preparations to you. I hope that all wise people will give instructions on the road construction and vehicle equipment at any time so as to achieve perfection. It is a great pleasure.

Shen Reported on the Construction Situation

Director Shen reported on the construction process. The Shanghai-Wuxi Road main line starts from Wuxi, passes through Changshu, Taicang, and Jiading counties, and reaches Shanghai, with a total length of about 140 kilometers. The length in Jiangsu is 130 kilometers, which is a major artery connecting the counties south of the Yangtze River to Shanghai. The branch line is from Changshu to Suzhou, with a mileage of 40 kilometers. Construction started in June last year and was completed in July this year. Now, I will report the summary of each project as follows: (1) Roadbed project: The width of the roadbed of the main line is 9 meters. Except for the Taicang section of the Taicang-Jiading section and the Jiading section of the Xiangzhen section, which have been built and only need to be repaired, the excavation and filling of the remaining earthwork is about 900,000 cubic meters. The width of the branch line is 7 meters, and the excavation and filling of the earthwork is about 500,000 cubic meters. (2) Bridge project: In addition to the original 22 bridges, 149 new bridges were built on the main line, with a total length of 2,080 meters. All of them are semi-permanent truss bridges, that is, the lower structure is made of reinforced concrete or stone masonry, and the upper part is made of wooden beams. Forty-five new bridges were built on the branch line, with a total length of 840 meters. (3) Culvert project: In addition to the original 30 culverts, 53 new reinforced concrete pipe culverts or stone masonry square culverts and 313 water pipes were built on the main line. Seventeen new culverts and 282 water pipes were built on the branch line, all in the same style as the main line. (4) Road surface project: The width of the road surface of the main line is temporarily 3 meters, which is a gravel road with a net length of 128 kilometers. When the subgrade is solid and there is a need for traffic, it will be widened and improved. The width of the branch line is 3 meters, which is a mud-bound crushed stone road with a net length of 39 kilometers. (5) Construction cost: The main line costs a total of 1.4 million yuan for new earthwork, bridges, culverts, pipes, and road surfaces. Among them, earthwork accounts for 10%, bridges account for 55%, road surfaces account for 25%, culverts and pipes account for 4%, and others account for 6%. The branch line costs a total of 500,000 yuan for new earthwork, bridges, culverts, and road surfaces. Among them, earthwork accounts for 10%, bridges and culverts account for 60%, road surfaces account for 20%, and others account for 10%. The total cost of the main and branch lines, excluding the original bridges, culverts, earthwork, and land prices, is about 2 million yuan. Among them, the Economic Committee allocated a loan of more than 289,000 yuan for construction costs, the Shanghai-Wuxi Long-Distance Motor Company allocated a loan of 744,000 yuan for construction costs, and paid a franchise driving security deposit of 68,000 yuan. The remaining amount was all allocated by Jiangsu Province. Thanks to the guidance and assistance of all parties and the joint efforts of the construction personnel, it was completed in one year. I am very grateful.

Wang Reported on the Company's Status

Wang Xiaolai, director of the Shanghai-Wuxi Company, reported that in order to save time, I will report on behalf of the company. Thank you all for coming from afar. The weather is very good today. It can be said that we have the right time, the right place, and the right people. The Yangtze River is to the north of this road, and the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway is to the south. The road is also very prosperous along the way. The road is jointly run by the government and the people, and everything can be done with sincerity and openness, resulting in good results. The motor company is a transportation agency. Domestic transportation is inconvenient. I hope that it can gradually develop to promote the development of culture and economy. Our company is commercial in nature, but we strive to reduce the car prices to serve the public. I hope that all sectors will give instructions to improve and achieve perfection.

Lunch and Sightseeing of Famous Scenic Spots

Arriving at the Shanghai-Wuxi Road, Changshu, it is a crossroads, with Wuxi to the west, Shanghai to the east, Suzhou to the south, and Changshu to the north. All guests got off the cars at the station. A temporary decorated archway was built there, with the words "Changshu County Government, County Party Department, and Various Organizations Welcome the Guests Participating in the Opening Ceremony" written on it. The number of Changshu people watching the excitement was no less than tens of thousands, which was rare in the past. All guests walked to the reception office on Nanjie Front Street for lunch. The hall of the Dadong Hotel was the reception office for foreign guests, the second floor was the rest area for female guests, and the second floor of the Deyi Building was the reception office. The upstairs of the Changle Tea Garden was the rest area for drivers and guards, and the second and third floors were the reception office. The second floor of the Greater China Tea House was the reception office for male guests. Lunch was all Changshu famous dishes from Shanjing Garden. After lunch, the guests visited Yushan Mountain. At the entrance of the mountain, the four big characters "Yushan Blessed Land" were written. (1) Yaji Pavilion: Located at the foot of the mountain west of the city, overlooking it, you can have a panoramic view of the scenery of the city. (2) Sword Gate: In front of the Fushui Temple, the mountain stone cliff is cracked like being split, with a cliff of more than ten feet, making people dare not look up. (3) Lianzhu Cave: Northwest of Poshang Temple, less than ten feet high, three feet wide, and four or five feet deep, the spring flows down from the stone hole and scatters like rain. (4) Taoyuan Ravine: There is a waterfall under the stone house ravine on the north mountain. (5) Tomb of Yanzi: East of Xiaosantai at the foot of the mountain in the county seat. (6) Weimo Temple: Above Shiwu Ravine, built in the first year of Longxing in the Song Dynasty. (7) Xukuo Residence: In Jiuwanwei in the county seat. (8) Fang Pagoda: Northeast of the county seat. (9) Fushui Rock: In front of Baoguo Temple on the top of the mountain. In addition, there are Poshan Xingfu, etc. After the participants enjoyed the tour, they took the original car back to Shanghai at 4:00 PM, which was already past 6:00 PM.

Japanese Aviator Aso Flew Back to His Country Yesterday Morning

United Press Agency, Omura, 15th - Japanese aviator Mr. Aso, who had been stranded in Shanghai by bad weather since arriving in Shanghai on the 4th of this month, finally had stable weather and took off from Shanghai at 7:45 AM on the 15th. He was met head-on by a northeast wind, and the difficult voyage continued. Therefore, it was much later than the scheduled time. When he flew to Kyushu, he was confused by the thick fog along the coast and failed to find the location of Ōtobase Airfield. Moreover, the gasoline ran out, so he had to land at the Omura Naval Airfield in Nagasaki Prefecture at 5:10 PM. He plans to spend the night here and fly to Tokyo tomorrow morning.

Dredging Bureau Requests Approval to Exempt Export Goods from Dredging Tax, Reduce the Burden on Merchants and Promote the Export of Local Goods; the Ministry Has Approved a Trial Period of One Year

Since Mr. Song Ziliang took office as the chief director of the Shanghai Dredging Bureau, he has spared no effort to develop port affairs and benefit merchants. Director Song believes that domestic commerce is declining and finance is exhausted. It is not enough to reverse the dangerous situation without finding ways to reduce the burden on merchants and encourage the increase in exports. Therefore, he requested the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance to approve the exemption of all dredging taxes levied on tax-free export goods and re-exported goods from Shanghai for a trial period of one year to see the effect. It is learned that the Bureau has received the joint order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating, "We have received the report that the request to exempt dredging donations on tax-free export goods and re-exported goods is to reduce the burden on merchants and encourage the export of local goods, which is feasible. It should be approved for a trial period, which will be implemented from August 1st. In addition to ordering the (Ministry of Finance) to instruct the customs to comply with the regulations, you should immediately comply with the regulations." It is also heard that this move by the Bureau will result in a significant loss in its regular revenue each year, but it is still willing to consider the difficulties of merchants, which is admirable.

Hydrographic Office Proclamation: There Are Submerged Reefs at the Mouth of the Xijiang River; Navigating Circles Must Pay Attention

The customs patrol ship Chaxing recently patrolled the coastal ports and discovered submerged reefs in the northwest of Dalanggang at the mouth of the Xijiang River, namely at 113 degrees 18 minutes east longitude and 21 degrees 59 minutes north latitude, 315 degrees from the top of Dalanggang Mountain, at a distance of about four chains. The reefs are already two feet above the water surface, which poses a significant hazard to navigation. It has been reported to the Hydrographic Office of the Ministry of the Navy to be included in the nautical chart, with dangerous lines and annotations such as "Two Feet Dry" and "Approximate Location" to alert the navigating circles to avoid misjudgment and accidents. The Hydrographic Office has issued Proclamation No. 136 to notify all shipping companies to inform their crew members to check and take note.

Continued Efforts in the Foreign Settlement to Prevent Cholera

According to a recent report submitted to the board of directors by the Public Works Department's health division, the sanitation conditions within the settlement were highly satisfactory until the end of June this year. However, with the sudden arrival of extreme heat in mid-July, a slight deterioration was observed, leading to instances of heatstroke, sudden collapses, and the occurrence of contagious gastrointestinal diseases, resulting in a number of fatalities. Nonetheless, the most notable feature of this year is the complete absence of cholera cases. Although there were reports of cholera cases in the newspapers last month, these were based on irresponsible rumors. Furthermore, the organizational structure of the agencies currently investigating cholera outbreaks is extremely thorough. Upon conducting on-site inspections, it can be immediately proven that these rumors are entirely unfounded. Regarding the measures taken by the health authorities in the foreign settlement to prevent cholera, they have adopted two approaches: one focusing on individuals and the other on drinking water. In terms of individual measures, over 49,000 people have already received preventative vaccinations this summer, not including the more than 2,200 individuals who received a second dose. As for drinking water, approximately 15,000 gallons of clean drinking water are supplied daily by the waterworks company to areas where clean water is lacking. In addition, the 972 drinking wells in the suburbs are disinfected on average every six days. Furthermore, strict attention is paid to street vendors selling cut fruit and iced drinks. Those who sell ice cream and fruit juices on the streets and markets without a license are subject to crackdown. People transporting ice cream are also required to wear badges to prevent impersonation. Several hundred bottles of privately made, uninspected fruit juice have also been seized and confiscated. Furthermore, the flytraps used by various beverage manufacturers last month have been highly effective and the health department has directed various food establishments and vegetable markets to adopt them extensively.

Loan Committee Actively Reviews Applications More Than Sixty Companies Apply For Loans Many Applicants Still Unclear About Procedures Not Only Do They Not Meet Regulations, but They Are Also Impossible to Review

Since the initiation of industrial and commercial credit loans in this city, some individuals have remained unclear about the true situation. Yesterday, our reporter specifically interviewed the person in charge of the loan review committee. According to him, the committee serves as an intermediary between the Ministry of Finance, the lending banks, and the borrowers. It hopes that all parties will cooperate sincerely to ensure smooth progress. If there are obstacles in the implementation of the loans, the committee will promptly propose to the Ministry of Finance methods to adapt to the environment. For example, the committee proposed to the Ministry of Finance to reduce the number of guarantors for credit loans from two shops to one, and to approve the dough industry association's method of joint and several guarantee. Lately, for the sake of the applicants, the committee is working with representatives of various banks to study the loan procedures, striving to make special accommodations within the realm of possibility. On the applicant side, the committee is also providing sincere guidance and has entrusted the accounting firm of Lisin to provide free guidance. However, most of the borrowers are small industrialists and businessmen, and their completed forms show that they have not previously had dealings with banks and money houses. They have little experience with business practices. This request for loans from the committee is like their first dealings with banks and money houses. Therefore, even with guidance, there are still many procedural errors, which not only fail to meet regulations but are also impossible to review. Although the committee is entrusted by the government to review loans, and has the nature of rescuing industry and commerce, it is not comparable to disaster relief. It cannot disregard regulations and make arbitrary loans in pursuit of the beautiful name of bestowing generosity and helping the masses. Currently, more than sixty companies have applied to the committee, and they are actively being investigated and reviewed. The committee will submit them to a meeting within days to decide on lending. However, the committee has entrusted the municipal chamber of commerce to issue more than four thousand blank application forms. There are many who have received the forms but have not yet applied. The reasons are nothing more than the following: (1) the Mid-Autumn Festival is not yet approaching, (2) difficulty in finding guarantors, (3) most lack business knowledge and are unclear about filling out the forms, (4) waiting and seeing. In addition to points (1) and (4), which are matters of time, there are remedies for points (2) and (3), as mentioned above. Therefore, the committee is always doing its best to achieve the goals of rescuing industry and commerce and stabilizing the market. It also hopes that those responsible for public opinion will clearly understand the committee's regulations and actual work situation, and provide reasonable supervision. If there are reasonable opinions, it is hoped that they will be contributed as much as possible so that the committee can forward them to the Ministry of Finance for adoption and implementation. Do not merely take passages out of context and make irrelevant criticisms, so as not to hinder the spirit of cooperation among all parties. In particular, it is hoped that assistance will be provided to guide borrowers who lack knowledge, as this is the most important point. It is like a doctor prescribing medicine, but if the patient does not know how to take it according to the prescription, it will ultimately be useless, and the responsibility is not entirely on the doctor. The letter from the committee to the municipal chamber of commerce regarding joint and several guarantees is extracted as follows: To: Municipal Chamber of Commerce Regarding your letter Shangzi No. 563, which stated that the Dough Industry Association requested that each member shop be given a loan according to the size of its capital, divided into several levels of one hundred yuan, fifty yuan, and thirty yuan, and that three shops would provide joint and several guarantees, and that the association would affix its seal to show credit, etc., requesting that the committee consider making changes to the regulations. Approved. The case has been resolved by the seventh meeting of the committee: "The requested small loans should be approved for modification to be guaranteed jointly and severally by three companies. Each industry association may also follow the example. After requesting instructions from the Ministry of Finance and obtaining approval, they will be approved for release." The minutes are on file. In addition to requesting instructions from the Ministry of Finance, a corresponding letter is hereby sent in reply. Please check and inform accordingly.

The Mainland Daily News reports that the annual report of the French Municipal Council was published on Wednesday (the 14th), totaling 600 pages. However, the amount of surplus from last year is more than this year, totaling 606,960.03 yuan. The income from various taxes is estimated to be 5,815,000 yuan, accounting for the majority of the income items. The rickshaw license tax is 410,000 yuan, and the private automobile license tax is 418,000 yuan. The annual report also contains information on the work done by various departments in 1934, with charts and photographs. The interest on various municipal bonds in 1934 amounted to a total of 1,766,915.93 yuan. The cost of maintaining hospitals in the French Concession was 260,302.645 yuan. The cost of municipal schools was 594,987.08 yuan. The salaries of the Municipal Council staff amounted to 4,103,277.78 yuan. The cost of maintaining parks was 3,148,190 yuan. The surplus for the 1934 special budget was 3,228,261.37 yuan, with income of 8,457,346.09 yuan and expenditure of 5,229,084.72 yuan.

At the end, the municipal party headquarters representative Ji Hao gave a speech, expressing his admiration for the union's spirit of unity and hoping that the elected members would carry forward the spirit of unity of the previous session. The General Union representative Shi Yitang also gave a speech. The meeting adjourned at 7 p.m.

This summer, the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have flooded, and all counties along the river in Anhui Province have suffered. Tongling County has the reputation of having three mountains and seven embankments. All large and small levees in the county are densely packed. For a month, they have been protected day and night. Unfortunately, the water level has increased day by day, and with the invasion of strong winds, more than 50 large and small embankments have collapsed, totaling over 90,000 mu of inundated farmland, with an estimated loss of over 800,000 yuan in agricultural products, more than 8,000 households of disaster victims, totaling more than 40,000 people, and 5,000 flooded houses, not to mention livestock and farming tools. In the past, when the Weixiang area was hit by a disaster, it could still seek food in the mountain areas. However, the mountain areas have not recovered from last year's severe drought and are unable to care for themselves. Now, the disaster victims are scattered and displaced, eating in the wind and sleeping in the open, crying out in a miserable way. As autumn approaches, we feel even more sorrow and pity. We are urgently seeking relief and jointly request that you allocate and distribute emergency relief to save the dying people." (2) A letter from the Shandong Yuncheng County Party Affairs Consolidation Committee states, "The people of Shanxi are unfortunate. For several years, disasters have been frequent, people's livelihoods have been exhausted, and the rural economy has collapsed. On July 10 of this year, the Yellow River burst its banks in Chenglingpu, and the rolling torrents directly flooded Yuncheng. Despite desperate efforts to block the breach, the water was too great to defend. The villages and fields that were flooded, houses were ruined, and miscellaneous supplies and food were all washed away. From the southern border of Shanxi to the northeastern border, a length of over 100 li and a width of 50-60 li, the water depth is 7-8 chi or 6-9 chi, a vast expanse of water, completely becoming a swamp. Of the nine districts in the county, eight have been affected. The number of villages affected is over 840, the number of disaster victims is over 300,000, and the loss of houses, equipment, food, etc. totals over 3 million yuan. The number of people and livestock who have died is still unknown. This is truly an unprecedented disaster for the people of Shanxi. All the flood victims are without food and clothing, and their cries are miserable to hear. The bodies of people and livestock are still being washed down the river from time to time. There are even bodies tied together in bundles of seven, eight, or even more than ten people. The sight is too terrible to see. The dead are gone, but what do the living rely on? The situation is dangerous, and relief is especially urgent. Please quickly allocate large sums to help the dying disaster victims."

Prediction by the Whangpoo Conservancy Board The Greatest High Tide This Morning Predicted to Exceed Twelve Feet and Still Rising

The high tide in the Whangpoo River at 0:40 yesterday morning also exceeded the amount predicted by the Whangpoo Conservancy Board, measuring 12 feet 3 inches (the prediction was 11 feet 9 inches). This high tide began to rise at 9:35 the night before last and did not completely recede until about 12:00 noon yesterday. According to the bureau's prediction, the highest tide of this month will occur at 1:20 this morning, measuring 12 feet 2 inches. However, based on the actual amounts recorded in the past two days, both have exceeded the predicted amounts, so the momentum will inevitably continue to increase. It is very close to the height of the 13-foot seawall at Outer Huangpu, which is worthy of attention. The following is a detailed list of the tide times: The high tide this morning began to rise at 11:40 last night. At 0:45 this morning, the rising trend was the most rapid, with a water flow rate of 2.2 nautical miles per hour. At 1:20, it reached its highest point, measuring 12 feet 2 inches (due to weather conditions, it will actually exceed this amount). It is expected to completely recede around noon today.

German Second Express Ship The Potsdam Arrives Today Enters Port at Twelve O'Clock Docks at Kung Ho Hsiang

The second new ship of the North German Lloyd, the Potsdam, arrived in Shanghai for the first time from Germany. Due to delays en route, it was ten days late. Yesterday, Messrs. Melchers & Co. received a wireless message from the captain of the ship stating that it would arrive off the Outer Tungsha sandbar in Wusong this morning, and a pilot had been assigned to guide it to Shanghai. It is expected that the Potsdam will reach the Whangpoo River around 12:00 noon, and passengers will disembark at the Kung Ho Hsiang wharf in Hongkou. The Potsdam has a net tonnage of 17,185 tons, a length of 193 meters, a width of 22.5 meters, and six decks. It is powered by electric turbines with a speed of 21 nautical miles per hour. The journey from Shanghai to Genoa takes 23 days.

Bank of China Employee Embezzles Huge Sum – Foolishly Takes 26,000 Yuan – Sentenced to Three Years in Prison After Interrogation

Chen Jixian, an employee of the payment department of the Hongkou branch of the Bank of China at 894 North Sichuan Road, was a native of Tongxiang, Zhejiang Province. On the afternoon of the 5th of this month, at 5:30 PM, he embezzled 26,000 yuan in silver notes and fled. The incident was reported to various police stations, and a reward was offered in newspapers for his arrest. However, there was no trace of him. It wasn't until 11 AM the day before yesterday that Wang Zhenfang, the manager of the branch, learned that Chen was hiding in the Shanghai Sanitarium at 150 Robber's Road, Hongkou. Wang then reported it to the Hongkou police station, which dispatched Chinese Detective Wang Chonghao and Western Detective with warrant No. 167 from Court No. 1, and secretly went to the hospital. They arrested him in room 26. The stolen money was found hidden in a small leather suitcase in the bathroom. Upon opening the door to the bathroom and inspecting the suitcase, they found 25,750 yuan of the original stolen money, leaving 250 yuan missing. Chen claimed that he gave 200 yuan to the hospital for fees and spent 50 yuan himself. Four keys and two seals were also found on his person and were taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, recounted the previous events, stating that the defendant had been working at the head office for four years. In March of this year, he was assigned to the Hongkou branch as a payment clerk. That evening, a shop owner named Wang Ruitang saw him lingering in the restroom for ten minutes before leaving with a hat box. The next day, the defendant sent a letter declaring his resignation. Now, according to Article 232, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, the crime of embezzlement in business is brought to public prosecution, and a severe sentence is requested. The evidence was presented for inspection. Wang Zhenfang, the head of the branch, also provided evidence. When questioned, the defendant confessed that unfortunately, something happened at home in his hometown, and he was burdened with many debts, which led his parents and wife into great difficulty. This caused him to suffer a nervous breakdown, leading him to resort to such a desperate measure, and he begged for leniency. Judge Xiao Xieffen sentenced Chen Jixian to three years in prison and a fine of 500 yuan. If the fine is commuted to labor service, it would be calculated at three yuan per day. The keys were confiscated, and the stolen money was returned to the original owner.

Public Works Department Health Inspection Office: Mortality Statistics for July. The Public Works Department's report for July stated that there were a total of 68 foreign residents born in the Public Concession that month, including 36 boys and 32 girls. There were a total of 796 Chinese residents born, including 411 boys and 385 girls. There were a total of 52 foreign residents who died that month, of which 23 were Japanese residents. The leading causes of death were pulmonary tuberculosis, heatstroke, heart disease, and tumors. A total of 1,420 Chinese residents died in July. The leading causes of death were weakness of old age, nervous system diseases, pulmonary tuberculosis, and intestinal diseases.

In July, there was a general increase in digestive system infections. A total of 8 foreigners and 69 Chinese suffered from major and minor injuries. 21 foreigners and 130 Chinese suffered from dysentery. In addition, two Chinese from outside the boundary died of hydrophobia at the Public Works Department's Chinese Isolation Hospital. One was a woman, age 31, who was bitten by a cat about three months prior. The other was a young man, age 27, who was bitten by a mad dog six weeks prior. Both died because they did not receive timely medical treatment.

Pushi Road: Counterfeit Silver Manufacturing Den Broken Up – Various Smelting Implements Arranged Neatly – Fourteen Workers and Shop Employees Detained

Jiang Futian, a detective inspector from the French Police, received a tip-off the day before yesterday, stating that at No. 117 Pushi Road (near the Sacred Heart Hospital), people were collecting double yuan silver coins and old items to melt and mix with lead to create silver bars and ingots for resale to small banks for profit, or so it was said, to be sold abroad. Inspector Jiang considered that damaging national currency violated the law. Based on the information, he reported it to the Western Detective Chief. On the morning of the 14th, at 3:00 AM, accompanied by Western Detective Chief Guli (transliteration), Liang Mu Wang Rusong, Zhang Daorong, Detectives Liu Jinrong, Guo Shaorong, Wang Dongwan, and other Chinese and Vietnamese police officers, they drove in police vehicles to No. 117 Pushi Road, the location of the operation. They first surrounded the building and then knocked on the door to enter. They found that the upper floors were all workshops, with various smelting and manufacturing implements arranged neatly. They arrested Ji Heshang from Shaoxing, Xie Laichao, Zhao Aquan, Zhou Shichao, Yu Qijin from Nantong, Yang Renchuan, Li Heshang, Zhou Guoan, Li Miaofa, Han Akang from the local area, Han Asheng, Wang Qingzhang from Ningbo, Liu A'er from Chongming, Chen Jianchu from Liuhou, Taicang, and 14 other people. These individuals were divided into workers responsible for melting, manufacturing, and other tasks, as well as tea servers, shop employees, and cooks. They confiscated 88 round silver lead blocks, 5 silver bricks, 12 lead bricks, as well as finished and unfinished blanks, and various equipment used for melting, with an estimated value of 300,000 to 400,000 yuan. They took all the witnesses and evidence back to the police station for investigation. They also dispatched detectives to guard the operation and arrest any remaining accomplices. After strict interrogation at the police station, the suspects confessed that the mastermind of the operation was Li Guoliang, a 26-year-old from Nantong, who lived at No. 364 Yongxing Road, Zhabei, and worked as the accountant in the Yichang Foundry. The front was run by Qi Runcai (age 33), the owner of the Wanshengxiang cigarette paper shop at No. 72 Huaxing Road, Zhabei, from Changshu. The French police immediately dispatched the original team of detectives to the Zhabei Public Security Bureau to request assistance in apprehending Li and Ni. The two suspects were arrested, and many privately manufactured silver bars were confiscated from their homes. They were taken to the Public Security Main Bureau for temporary detention. Yesterday, due to the Catholic Feast of the Assumption, the French Police Department was closed for the holiday and did not work, so they could not be sent to court. The 14 suspects arrested on Pushi Road will be sent to the Second Special Court this morning for questioning. At the same time, they will request the court to prepare a document to transfer Li and Ni from the Public Security Bureau to their custody for questioning. On Binlang Road, four robbers from Jiangbei, Cao Youxian, Yin Zixiang, Li Wangshi, and Liu Beipei, were arrested. Two handguns and 19 bullets were confiscated and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special Court with a request for detention pending investigation. Zhang Tianyin, a lawyer from the police station, rose and detailed the circumstances of the case, stating that on the morning of the 13th of this month, at 12:15 AM, Chinese Detective Inspector Qi Mengqing received a tip-off that a gang of thieves was hiding at No. 5 Junyi Lane, Binlang Road in the Chinese area, intending to rob the wealth of the St. Anna Dance Hall opposite the Zhaofeng Garden in West Shanghai that night. He, along with police detectives from the Sixth District Public Security Bureau, went to the address. Upon entering the room, they found Cao and Yin sleeping in the same bed and arrested them. They confiscated two handguns, 19 bullets, and two magazines from under the pillow, along with the woman Li Wangshi, and took them to the Public Security Bureau. Shortly after, Liu Depei arrived at the house and was apprehended by the Public Security Bureau officers guarding the house and transferred to the police station. When questioned about the source of the handguns, Cao Youxian confessed that the guns and bullets belonged to Sun Daerzi, who lived in Huazibang, Zhabei. The detectives went to arrest Sun, but he had already fled. They only confiscated a string of fake pearls. Then, based on Cao's confession, they arrested an accomplice named Wang in a bungalow on Guangfu Road, but he had also escaped. They confiscated a pawn ticket and retrieved a watch from a pawnshop. After investigation, they learned that the fake pearls and watch were the original stolen goods from the Zhao family at No. 25, Lane 49, Zhoujia Bridge Road, robbed at 8:00 AM on June 23rd of this year. The two confiscated handguns had also been sent to the Public Works Department for inspection. One of the handguns, No. [illegible], was found to be related to the robbery of a resident at No. 10 Dongjiatan, Yinxiang Port, at 2:00 AM on December 9th of last year, and the robbery and attempted murder of a resident at No. 143 Tangshan Road at 3:00 AM on April 3rd of this year. Since the investigation of this case is not yet complete, he requested permission to detain the suspects. It was also found that Cao Youxian, Yin Zixiang, and Liu Depei had all been convicted of theft. Cao was sentenced to 15 years in prison in the Chinese area, Yin was sentenced to 10 years in this court, and Liu was sentenced to 5 years in the French Concession. All three were repeat offenders. The four suspects all denied the charges. Judge Wu Zehan reviewed the confessions and approved the detention of the four defendants for seven days pending further investigation.

Five Murder Cases Occur in Nanshi, Zhabei, and West Shanghai

Five murder cases occurred in Nanshi, Zhabei, West Shanghai, and other areas of the city in the past two days. The police stations have assigned local heads to report to the local court for corpse examination. The details of each case are listed below:

Died from Vomiting Blood: Wen Yuhong from Yangzhou, age 53, residing at No. 16 Yuelai Street, Xiaodongmen, Yuchangshou's residence, had been unemployed for a long time. Unexpectedly, at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, he suddenly vomited blood profusely on the way on Yuelai Street. His complexion changed rapidly, and he collapsed to the ground, barely breathing. When the police from Post No. 19 of the 16th Sub-bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Fang Yulong, discovered the situation and rushed to investigate, he had already died. The incident was reported to Director Huang Junfu, who submitted a report to the General Bureau for filing. The local head was instructed to report to the court for a corpse examination. The deceased had no family members, only a friend named Luo Chunshan, who lives at the Garbage Bridge in the Public Concession.

Died in a Car from Illness: Ye Xianmei from Taizhou, Zhejiang, age 38, residing at No. 30 Wujiazhai, Jisi Feier Road, West Shanghai, made socks for a living. Ye had recently been ill and had no money for treatment. After borrowing a few yuan, he took a rickshaw to seek medical treatment at around 8:00 AM yesterday morning. Unexpectedly, when the rickshaw arrived at the entrance of the alley, Ye suddenly deteriorated and died inside the rickshaw. The police officer from the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau in West Shanghai noticed the situation and reported it to Inspector Long, who reported it to Sub-bureau Director Tan Baoshou. A report was submitted to the General Bureau for filing. The local head was instructed to report to the court for a corpse examination.

Hanging Himself Over a Dispute: Li Gendao, a local, age 36, lived in Guchazhai No. 14, Pengpei Town, and made a living by farming. At around 8:00 AM yesterday morning, he had a dispute with his elder brother, Li Rongfeng, who lived next door, over the problem of a thatched shed. After Gendao was reprimanded by Rongfeng, he turned and went home, harboring resentment and a desire to end his life. Late at night, he sneaked to the doorway of Li Rongfeng's house and hanged himself. A neighbor discovered the body and reported it to the Pupu Outpost of the Xinzha Sub-bureau of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who reported it to the General Bureau for filing. The local head was instructed to report to the local court for a corpse examination.

Suicide Due to Quarrel: Zhu, who resided at No. 8 Youche Lane, Youche Wharf, Nanshi, married a woman surnamed Wang from Zhenhai, Zhejiang, last year (namely, Zhu Wangshi, age 19). After the marriage, the relationship between the couple was harmonious. Unexpectedly, the woman became upset with her husband over a minor matter the night before last, and secretly hanged herself. Her elder brother, Wang Rongding, discovered the body and tried to save her, but it was too late. He reported the incident to Dongjiadu Police Station Chief Yi Zuanshi, who sent Inspector Chen to investigate and reported the incident to the General Bureau.

Suicide Due to Stupidity: Jiang Jinhai (age 26, from Tongzhou), a colleague of Zhu Shengshi, who ran the Zhu Shunxing Copper Workshop at No. 17 Minzhu Street, Lao Beimen, was recently studying at the literacy school at No. 33 Lane, Houjia Road. However, Jiang Jinhai had a poor memory and found it difficult to write down the new characters taught each day. If he was asked to recite them, he would stare blankly and be unable to answer. Therefore, he felt sorry for himself. The night before last, while his colleagues were asleep, he hanged himself with lead wire on the mezzanine. It was not until about 5:00 AM yesterday morning that a colleague noticed the body and was shocked. He tried to untie the rope, but the body was already cold as ice. He reported it to the police station, instructing the ninth-district head, Jiang Pingyang, to report to the local court for an examination. It was also stated that Professor Wang Baoliang from the school had said that the deceased had not attended classes for several days. After receiving the report, the court immediately appointed Prosecutor Ouyang Shu and Examiner Xuan Zhiming to conduct an on-site examination and confirm the death.

Brother Stabs Sister-in-Law to Death: A Bizarre Case of Family Misfortune

Yue Zihong, age 21, who worked as a peddler, was from Shanghai. His elder brother, Zicheng, age 38, also worked as a peddler. The two brothers lived together at No. 12 Jukui South Lane, Jukui Street, Xiaodongmen. The brothers got along well on weekdays. They set up a stall at the street entrance, selling toys, and their lives were not bad. In December of last year, Zihong married a woman surnamed Shen (17 years old this year) from Changzhou with the help of a matchmaker. The couple's relationship was harmonious. Unexpectedly, Ms. Shen suddenly ran away from home without her husband's knowledge in April of this year. The Caojiadu Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau arrested her and transferred her to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. Her husband, Yue Zihong, was then summoned to take custody of her. After Yue Zihong brought Ms. Shen back home, she suddenly said that her brother-in-law, Zicheng, had repeatedly flirted with her, and she ran away because she couldn't stand it. At around 8:00 AM yesterday morning, Zihong went out to sell toys. However, his elder brother, Zicheng, was sick at home. Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 AM, Zicheng suddenly jumped out of bed, took a triangular, sharp knife about eight inches long, and ran into Ms. Shen's room. He suddenly stabbed Ms. Yue Pan's left chest below the breast, about several inches deep. Ms. Pan screamed in pain and fell to the ground, blood gushing out like a spring. Zicheng's anger did not subside. He stabbed Ms. Pan's lower body three or four more times. Realizing that he had committed a serious crime, he hurriedly ran down the stairs. At this time, the second landlord of the house, Ms. Gao, suddenly heard a desperate cry for help from the Yue's room upstairs. Knowing that something was wrong, she immediately went upstairs to investigate and met Yue Zicheng. She only saw him rushing downstairs and did not know what had happened. When Ms. Gao went upstairs and saw Ms. Pan lying in a pool of blood, unable to speak, she was shocked. She immediately called the neighbors in the house to help chase after Zicheng. At that time, Zicheng had already fled out the door and disappeared. She immediately called Ms. Pan's husband, Yue Zihong, to report the incident to the Chenghuang Temple Police Station, who immediately dispatched an inspector to investigate. Ms. Pan had already died. A bloodstained murder weapon was found in the room and taken back to the station. The incident was reported to Director Liu of the police station. Considering that the case involved human life and the circumstances were bizarre, he instructed the local head to report to the local court and send someone to conduct an on-site examination. He also ordered the police to pay attention and investigate the suspect in the case and bring him to justice. After this case occurred, it spread far and wide, so many people went to watch, and Jukui Street was very crowded.

Woman's Lapse Kills Apprentice: Boat Moves Straight Outward – Apprentice Loses Footing and Falls into River

Yongning Lane No. 23 Hankou Road, Qufeng Store, yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, sent eight partners and apprentices to Longmao Dock, Lujiazui, Pudong, to pack the white cotton into foreign parcels, in order to sell them at the pier. At 12:05 PM, they hired a No. 1515 rowboat to cross the river. When they arrived at the Wuma Road dock in Puxi, the boatwoman Zhang Shi used her hand to pull the pier's outer fender. The people got ashore one after another, and the last apprentice, Xia Pengnian, was about to follow when Shi suddenly loosened her hands and the rowboat moved straight outward. Xia lost his footing and fell into the river on the spot. Although the people on the shore threw life buoys, it was impossible to save him, and Xia was submerged and disappeared. The partners reported to the Customs Water Police Station, who sent detectives to take the two women Zhang Shi and Yang Ma to the police station and asked them why they had fled and failed to rescue him. However, the two women suddenly pointed out that the deceased had jumped into the river to commit suicide. Considering that the case involved human life, they were instructed to wait for the court to investigate this morning. It is reported that the deceased was 16 years old, from Shaoxing, and was the only son. His family only had a mother, which is extremely tragic.

Man and Woman Commit Suicide by Poison at Hongkou Hotel – Man Dead, Woman in Critical Condition

A stylish young woman with short hair and leather shoes, dressed smartly, arrived at the Hongkou Hotel on North Sichuan Road the day before yesterday at 11:00 AM. She looked to be in her twenties and spoke with a Cantonese accent. She called herself Ms. He and asked for a room. The room service attendant led her to room 94. In the evening, a young man entered the room and talked for a long time. Later, they closed the door and there was no movement. The next day, the room service attendant discovered that a man and a woman had committed suicide by poison in room 94. They managed to pry open the door and saw the man and woman sleeping together under a quilt, looking pale. They found an empty bottle of Lysol and knew that they had been poisoned. They reported it to the cashier, who reported it to the police station. An ambulance was called, and the man was sent to Tongren Hospital, but he had taken too much poison and died soon after. The woman was sent to the Shanghai Sanitarium on Bazilu Road for treatment. At midnight, she was still in critical condition.

Then all the people who proposed to her went to buy lottery tickets, not only to win the prize, but also to marry Ayun. When Xiangsheng learned about this method, he was naturally a little sad, but after Ayun explained it to him, he understood that Ayun was marrying the country for the sake of righteousness, so how could he bear to take this "Wife of the Republic of China" as his own?

Our Nation's Cinnamon: Can Be Used to Produce High-Quality Essences - Recent Invention by a French Technician - Ministry of Industry Orders Promotion of Planting

China News Agency reports that our nation's cinnamon, produced in Yunnan, Guizhou, and various border counties of Guangdong and Guangxi, is cultivated both artificially and naturally. The annual total output accounts for 65% of the world's total. Since the opening of trade, sales have been very brisk, but it has only been used as a medicinal tonic. Recently, a French perfume chemist invented a method to produce special essences, which are a major ingredient for various high-quality perfumes, soaps, and face powders. Not only is the fragrance pure and rich, but it can also maintain the aroma of other mixtures and prevent them from dissipating. Therefore, recent sales have been increasingly active. After the International Trade Bureau reported this to the Ministry of Industry, in addition to ordering the relevant departments in the four provinces to actively promote planting, it also ordered the bureau to continue to pay attention to overseas promotion efforts.

Zhong Hang Sikorsky Plane Sunk: Retrieved Yesterday and Soon to be Shipped to Shanghai - Whether it can Still be Used Depends on Inspection - Luoning No. 4 Plane Also Shipped to Shanghai for Repair

The Sikorsky plane of China Aviation Corporation, parked at the Hankou seaplane airport, had its pontoon chains broken by a sudden hurricane in Hankou on the 13th afternoon, causing it to collide with the No. 2 Luoning plane. Due to the strong winds, the wings of both planes were damaged. The Sikorsky plane was severely damaged and was immediately swept into the water by the waves. The Luoning plane only suffered damage to its left wing. According to yesterday's news from China Aviation Corporation, after the wind collision occurred, in addition to immediately reporting to the Ministry of Transportation, the Hankou branch was instructed to find a way to salvage the sunken plane and ship it to Shanghai for repair along with the damaged Luoning plane. The company received a telegram from Hankou yesterday stating that the Sikorsky plane had been salvaged from the water at noon yesterday. The extent of the damage and whether it can still be used will be determined after a detailed inspection in Shanghai. The damaged plane and the other plane will arrive in the next day or two. It is also reported that the Sikorsky plane that was sunk this time is a biplane amphibious aircraft, the same as the one that was previously destroyed near Zhenhai. It has two engines and is worth more than 100,000 yuan.

Japanese Hakutaka Warship to Hong Kong Tomorrow - Fisheries Training Class of the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry Conducts Deep-Sea Fishing Practice

The Fisheries Training Institute of the Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, due to the graduation of all its students, has dispatched the training warship Hakutaka, commanded by Captain Jinzo Nakagawa, carrying 15 instructors from the Fisheries Training Institute and 31 graduates from the Fisheries Department of the Training Institute, to conduct deep-sea practice, departing from Japan on May 13. They first sailed from Hokkaido and other places, then to Vladivostok, and then to the seas off Korea, Lushun, and Dalian to practice new fishing methods. Finally, they arrived in Qingdao and then came to Shanghai from Jiaozhou, arriving on the day before yesterday, after three months. After the ship's instructors and students arrived in Shanghai, they were busy with banquets hosted by Japanese officials and civilians in Shanghai. Yesterday, the students also inspected Shanghai, paying close attention to our country's fishing market. It is now scheduled to depart from Shanghai tomorrow (the 17th) at 4 PM on the original warship Hakutaka, first to Hong Kong, then to Taiwan, and then back to Japan. When the ship leaves Shanghai, it will also practice fishing and other techniques in the waters outside Wusongkou and the Zhoushan Islands.

The Traffic Department of the China Electric Company, for the convenience of traffic and passengers, has decided that the Route 3 tram stop, originally located at the Fu'an Company on Dongmen Road, will be moved because of the installation of traffic lights at that location, which is inconvenient for passengers getting on and off. Article 9: In addition to participating themselves, founders who can introduce others to join should notify in writing at any time. Article 10: These regulations shall not apply from the time the Founders' Meeting establishes the Preparatory Committee and selects its members.

Ciyou Association and Hudong Public Society Jointly Organize: Graduation Ceremony Held at Nursery School - Today at 5 PM - Total of 12 Graduating Children

On April 1, 1933, the China Ciyou Association and the Hudong Public Society, recognizing that the Yangshupu area is filled with factories and that female workers are burdened by work and have difficulty caring for their children, which is detrimental to the children's well-being, jointly established the Shanghai Ciyou Nursery School at 1519 Yangshupu Bridge to alleviate the suffering of workers, assist them in raising their children, and increase their work efficiency. The school's organization is divided into two departments: infant and kindergarten. The infant department admits boys and girls aged two to four, and the kindergarten department admits boys and girls aged four to six. Workers who work in factories and cannot take care of their children can fill out a request form and entrust their children to the school. Children are sent to the school by their families at 10:00 AM every day (except Sundays) and picked up at 5:00 PM. Lunch and afternoon snacks are provided by the school. The education of children focuses on scientific childcare and enlightening teaching. The environment is beautiful and the equipment is suitable. The school's teachers visit the children's families once a week and hold a parent-teacher conference once a month to establish close contact and cooperation with the children's families. Since its establishment nearly two and a half years ago, it has been widely praised by the general working class due to its perfect management and outstanding achievements. Today (the 16th) at 5:00 PM, the school will hold its third graduation ceremony, with a total of 12 graduating children. The school has sent out invitations to various circles to visit and guide the event. The reporter has investigated and recorded the order of the meeting as follows: (1) The chairman announces the opening of the meeting and conducts the ceremony. (2) Opening remarks (Mr. Qiu Zidong, President of the Hudong Public Society). (3) Sing the Children's Year Song (all children). (4) Speech (Mr. Chen Zhengfan, staff member of the China Ciyou Association). (5) Sing the Graduation Song (all graduates). (6) Issuance of diplomas and awards (Dr. Qiu Zidong). (7) Admonition (Dr. Qiu Zidong). (8) Graduation speech (Hu Genrong). (9) Appreciation speech from the children's families (Zheng Zhongai, Ruan Xingye, Chen Bangzhong). (10) Photography. (11) Tea party. (12) Adjournment. It is expected that the nursery profession will be so perfect and there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Brief Discussion on Lotus Blooming in Gu Garden

The lotus pond in Gu Garden, located west of Kunshan Station and east of Zhenyi Station on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, has been known for its precious double-blooming lotus seeds for hundreds of years. After the descendants of the Gu family and celebrities such as Ye Gongchuo and Ren Xiaoshan jointly organized a management committee with the gentry of Zhenyi Town, they engaged in renovations. This spring, the committee opened another pond next to the original lotus pond and sought seeds of white lotus that had been growing for hundreds of years from the Wei family's garden west of the town and planted them there. As a result, this year's blooming of red and white lotus flowers is more magnificent than in previous years. The white lotus flowers each bloom with a single flower, which is as large as a large bowl, while the red lotus flowers, in addition to the double-blooming lotus (two flowers per stem) and the four-faced Guanyin (four flowers per stem), have up to nine flowers blooming on each stem, resembling peony flowers from afar. As a result, people from Shanghai, Hangzhou, Suzhou, Kunshan, and other places have come to visit and admire the flowers every day. It is said that the Ministry of Railways installed dozens of white stone chairs around the pond this year for visitors to rest. However, Xiao Wuxi, the worker who manages the pond and pavilion, took this opportunity to prepare tea and snacks for visitors to taste and drink, and his business has tripled since the lotus flowers bloomed. It is also said that the Wang Kai Photo Studio in Shanghai recently sent photographers to the countryside to take many films of the famous flowers for display in Shanghai.

Woman Casts Herself into the River Due to Grievances

Zhang Quanmei, a young woman of 21 from Liyang, lived at 34 Minghua Fang, Tilanqiao, Huishan Road. Last month, her husband had her transport more than a hundred dan of rice back to Liyang for sale. After selling all the rice, she received more than 500 yuan in banknotes, which she hid in her handbag. She stayed at an inn that night, but at 11:00 PM, an acquaintance, someone named Jia, knocked on the door and entered to chat. Taking advantage of the opportunity, he stole her handbag, which contained the banknotes, a pair of gold bracelets, two gold rings, and a watch. When Zhang Quanmei discovered the theft, he had already disappeared. After returning to Shanghai, her husband did not believe her and beat and scolded her, causing her to become increasingly resentful and world-weary. The night before last, she left alone and walked to the Bund on Nanjing Road after midnight. She jumped into the river in an attempt to commit suicide. The sound of her jump alerted two sampan men nearby, who immediately went to rescue her. She was sent to the Customs Water Police Station, where she explained the reason for her suicide and claimed that she had swallowed a gold ring before jumping into the river. The police chief, seeing that she was determined to die, immediately summoned her husband to the police station and persuaded him. The two were sent to the local court yesterday morning, and the court was asked to request the Liyang government to arrest the original thief and investigate the matter.

Revised and Promulgated Fishing Regulations for Hongkou Park

The fishing regulations for Hongkou Park have been revised and promulgated by the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council and will take effect on September 1. Anyone intending to fish there must abide by the regulations and first apply to the Public Works Department of the Municipal Council for a license. The license fee is three yuan per year, excluding the park entrance fee. Each person is limited to one fishing rod and two fish per day. Any fish exceeding two or less than six inches long must be released back into the pond and cannot be taken away. Unnecessary harm to the fish is also prohibited. There are a total of eight such regulations. Anyone who violates or violates the regulations will have their license revoked by the Municipal Council at any time.

Overview of Milk Inspection in the Public Concession in July

The Health Department of the Municipal Council reported that the average milk production in the city in July was divided among 13 companies. The average daily production of milk cheese was 637 pounds, and the average daily production of milk oil was 86 pounds, both of which were lower than the previous month. This month, 11 types of milk samples failed to meet chemical standards, and 35 out of 89 types failed to meet microbial standards. Six cows died from pleuropneumonia, one cow died from infectious carbuncle, six cows died from pulmonary tuberculosis, and 14 cows died from other diseases in the milk sheds. In total, 29 cows died this month. This month, 136 animals belonging to Grade A pastures were tested for pulmonary tuberculosis upon request, and the heads showed a reaction and were immediately isolated.

An Incident in Purchasing the Song Dynasty Collection

Yunnan is remote and far away, but the people are very devout Buddhists. Abbot Haimen of Jianquan Temple in Shun Ning, who is diligent in practice and constantly striving, is especially respected by the public. Previously, he heard that the photoprinted Song Dynasty Qisha edition of the Great Tibetan Sutra was being sold in Shanghai. He made a special wish to purchase a copy for the temple, saving on food and clothing and mortgaging farmland to obtain 1,300 Yunnan coins, equivalent to 545 Shanghai coins, and entrusted the Kunming Changmeili Company to remit the funds for purchase. However, the company delayed for three years and embezzled the funds, failing to remit them. Abbot Haimen had no choice but to present the situation to the magistrate of Shun Ning County, who was greatly angered and has requested the mayor of Kunming to strictly pursue the recovery of the funds in order to fulfill the initial wish of completing the canon.

Guangdong Opera at Mingzhu Grand Theater Opens Tonight: The Feng Laiyi Troupe, a famous Guangdong opera troupe that was hired by the Mingzhu Grand Theater on Fusheng Road, has already arrived in Shanghai. It is said that the troupe includes famous actors Liang Shaochu and Kunqu opera singer Xiao Lifei, who are skilled and have a reputation in the Pearl River. The theater's playwright, Lei Gong, has a close friendship with these performers and has agreed to come to Shanghai to perform. Lovers of Guangdong opera should definitely be eager to see them.
